Get Started

Welcome to Helius

We’re building the infrastructure for the world’s first global financial computer. Whether you’re building the next DeFi protocol, creating innovative NFT experiences, or pioneering entirely new financial primitives, Helius gives you the tools to turn ambitious ideas into reality. We don’t settle for “good enough”—we build infrastructure that entire markets depend on. ![Helius Hero](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/images/hero-light.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=7e0eb2c7834f3536307c78ec3eec41bb)

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs#start-building-with-helius)

API Reference

Authentication

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#authentication)

Authentication
==============================================================================================

Helius API uses API keys to authenticate requests. Every API request must include your API key to verify your identity and permissions.

Your API key is sensitive information that grants access to your Helius account. Never expose it in client-side code, public repositories, or browser-accessible areas.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#getting-started)

Getting Started
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#1-create-your-api-key)

1\. Create Your API Key

1

Sign up or log in

Create an account on the [Helius Dashboard](https://dashboard.helius.dev/)
 or log in to your existing account.

2

Navigate to API Keys

Go to the **API Keys** section in your dashboard sidebar.

3

Generate a new key

Click **Create New API Key** and provide a descriptive name for your project (e.g., “Production App”, “Development Environment”).

4

Copy and secure your key

Copy your API key immediately and store it securely. You won’t be able to see it again once you navigate away.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#2-using-your-api-key)

2\. Using Your API Key

Include your API key as a query parameter in all requests:

cURL

JavaScript

Python

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    curl "https://mainnet.helius-rpc.com/?api-key=YOUR_API_KEY" \
      -X POST \
      -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
      -d '{"jsonrpc":"2.0","id":1,"method":"getAccountInfo","params":["ACCOUNT_ADDRESS"]}'
    

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#security-best-practices)

Security Best Practices
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment Variables
---------------------

Store your API key in environment variables, not in your source code.

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    export HELIUS_API_KEY="your-api-key-here"
    

IP Restrictions
---------------

Set up IP restrictions for your API keys in the dashboard to limit access to specific IP addresses or ranges.

Separate Keys
-------------

Use different API keys for development, staging, and production environments to isolate usage and improve security.

Monitor Usage
-------------

Regularly check your API usage in the dashboard to detect unusual patterns or potential security issues.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#secret-management)

Secret Management

*   Node.js
    
*   Python
    
*   Docker
    

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    // Use environment variables
    const apiKey = process.env.HELIUS_API_KEY;
    
    // Or use a secrets manager
    const { SecretManagerServiceClient } = require('@google-cloud/secret-manager');
    const client = new SecretManagerServiceClient();
    
    async function getApiKey() {
      const [version] = await client.accessSecretVersion({
        name: 'projects/PROJECT_ID/secrets/helius-api-key/versions/latest',
      });
      return version.payload.data.toString();
    }
    

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    import os
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
    
    # Load environment variables
    load_dotenv()
    api_key = os.getenv('HELIUS_API_KEY')
    
    # Or use AWS Secrets Manager
    import boto3
    
    def get_secret():
        client = boto3.client('secretsmanager')
        response = client.get_secret_value(SecretId='helius-api-key')
        return response['SecretString']
    

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    # In your Dockerfile
    ENV HELIUS_API_KEY=""
    
    # Or use Docker secrets
    RUN --mount=type=secret,id=helius_key \
        cat /run/secrets/helius_key > /app/api_key.txt
    

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#rate-limits-&-usage)

Rate Limits & Usage
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Rate limits vary by subscription plan. Monitor your usage in the [Helius Dashboard](https://dashboard.helius.dev/)
 to ensure you stay within your allocated limits.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#understanding-rate-limits)

Understanding Rate Limits

*   **Requests per second**: Based on your subscription tier
*   **Monthly request quota**: Total requests allowed per billing cycle
*   **Burst allowance**: Short-term spikes above your base rate limit

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#handling-rate-limits)

Handling Rate Limits

JavaScript

Python

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    async function makeRequest(url, data) {
      try {
        const response = await fetch(url, {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
        
        if (response.status === 429) {
          const retryAfter = response.headers.get('Retry-After');
          console.log(`Rate limited. Retry after ${retryAfter} seconds`);
          await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, retryAfter * 1000));
          return makeRequest(url, data); // Retry
        }
        
        return response.json();
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Request failed:', error);
        throw error;
      }
    }
    

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/authentication#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Invalid API Key Error

**Symptoms**: 401 Unauthorized or “Invalid API Key” errors**Solutions**:

*   Verify your API key is correct and hasn’t been regenerated
*   Check that you’re including the API key as a query parameter: `?api-key=YOUR_KEY`
*   Ensure there are no extra spaces or characters in your API key
*   Confirm your API key hasn’t expired or been revoked

Rate Limit Exceeded

**Symptoms**: 429 Too Many Requests errors**Solutions**:

*   Check your current usage in the dashboard
*   Implement exponential backoff in your retry logic
*   Consider upgrading your plan for higher limits
*   Optimize your requests to reduce unnecessary calls

Forbidden Access

**Symptoms**: 403 Forbidden errors**Solutions**:

*   Verify IP restrictions aren’t blocking your requests
*   Check that your subscription includes access to the endpoint
*   Ensure your API key has the necessary permissions

API 参考

Solana API 参考：完整列表

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference#solana-rpc-api)

Solana RPC API

[HTTP 方法\
-------\
\
有效地进行交易，立即查询区块链数据，并受益于增强的可靠性和性能。](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/rpc/http-methods)
[WebSocket 方法\
------------\
\
通过订阅实时区块链事件创建响应式应用程序。消除轮询并减少用户界面的延迟。](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/rpc/websocket-methods)

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference#%E4%BB%A3%E5%B8%81%E4%B8%8E%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93-api)

代币与交易 API

[数字资产标准 (DAS)\
------------\
\
通过单个 API 调用访问标准化的代币和 NFT 元数据。自动处理常规和压缩的 NFT。](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/das)
[优先费用 API\
--------\
\
根据当前网络状况获取推荐的交易费用。防止超时并确保交易的及时确认。](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/priority-fee/getpriorityfeeestimate)
[增强交易\
----\
\
以人类可读的格式检索预解析的交易数据。通过结构化信息节省开发时间，准备好显示。](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/enhanced-transactions)
[ZK 压缩\
-----\
\
将链上数据的账户存储成本显著降低至 98%。](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/zk-compression)

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference#%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E6%B5%81-api)

数据流 API

[LaserStream gRPC\
----------------\
\
使用轻量级客户端以超低延迟流式传输区块链数据。应用自定义过滤器以仅接收与您的应用程序相关的更新。](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/laserstream-grpc)

[Webhooks\
--------\
\
配置直接发送到您的应用程序的区块链事件即时通知。消除持续轮询的需要，同时保持数据的时效性。](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/webhooks)

Digital Asset Standard (DAS)

Digital Asset Standard (DAS)

[getAsset\
--------\
\
Retrieves information about a specific asset by its ID.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getasset)
[getAssetBatch\
-------------\
\
Retrieves information about multiple assets in a single request.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getassetbatch)
[getAssetProof\
-------------\
\
Fetches a proof for a specific compressed asset.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getassetproof)
[getAssetProofBatch\
------------------\
\
Fetches proofs for multiple compressed assets in a single request.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getassetproofbatch)
[getAssetsByAuthority\
--------------------\
\
Returns assets by the specified authority address.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getassetsbyauthority)
[getAssetsByCreator\
------------------\
\
Retrieves assets created by a specific creator address.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getassetsbycreator)
[getAssetsByGroup\
----------------\
\
Returns assets that belong to a specific group.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getassetsbygroup)
[getAssetsByOwner\
----------------\
\
Lists all assets owned by a specific address.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getassetsbyowner)
[getNftEditions\
--------------\
\
Retrieves information about NFT editions.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getnfteditions)
[getSignaturesForAsset\
---------------------\
\
Returns transaction signatures involving a specific asset.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getsignaturesforasset)
[getTokenAccounts\
----------------\
\
Retrieves token accounts based on specified parameters.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/gettokenaccounts)
[searchAssets\
------------\
\
Searches for assets based on various criteria.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/searchassets)

[getAssetRetrieve comprehensive data for any Solana NFT or digital asset by its unique identifier. This endpoint provides complete on-chain and off-chain metadata, ownership details, royalty information, collection data, and compression state for any Solana digital asset. The getAsset method supports all token standards including compressed NFTs (cNFTs), programmable NFTs (pNFTs), and traditional SPL tokens. Use this endpoint to: - Fetch complete metadata for NFT marketplace listings - Retrieve asset ownership information for wallet integrations - Access royalty and creator data for royalty enforcement - Check compression status to identify cost-efficient compressed NFTs - View collection grouping for NFT collection analytics\

API Reference

Solana API Reference: Complete List

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference#solana-rpc-apis)

Solana RPC APIs

[HTTP Methods\
------------\
\
Land transactions effectively, query blockchain data instantly, and benefit from enhanced reliability and performance.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/rpc/http-methods)
[WebSocket Methods\
-----------------\
\
Create responsive applications by subscribing to real-time blockchain events. Eliminate polling and reduce latency in your user interfaces.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/rpc/websocket-methods)

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference#token-&-transaction-apis)

Token & Transaction APIs

[Digital Asset Standard (DAS)\
----------------------------\
\
Access standardized token and NFT metadata with a single API call. Handles both regular and compressed NFTs automatically.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das)
[Priority Fee API\
----------------\
\
Get recommended transaction fees based on current network conditions. Prevent timeouts and ensure timely confirmation of your transactions.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/priority-fee/getpriorityfeeestimate)

---------------------\
\
Retrieve pre-parsed transaction data in human-readable format. Save development time with structured information ready for display.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/enhanced-transactions)

--------------\
\
Dramatically reduce account storage costs by up to 98% for on-chain data.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/zk-compression)

Data Streaming APIs

----------------\
\
Stream blockchain data with ultra-low latency using lightweight clients. Apply custom filters to receive only the updates relevant to your application.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/laserstream-grpc)

[Webhooks\
--------\
\
Configure instant notifications for blockchain events sent directly to your application. Eliminate the need for constant polling while maintaining data currency.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/webhooks)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When Reporting Technical Issues
-------------------------------

1.  Your Project ID
2.  Request details (endpoint, parameters)
3.  Error messages or response codes
4.  Timestamps of when the issue occurred

# Shred Delivery - Helius Docs

[跳转到主要内容](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/shred-delivery#content-area)

New: getTransactionsForAddress - Query transaction history with advanced filtering, sorting, and pagination. [Learn More](https://www.helius.dev/docs/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

New: getTransactionsForAddress - Query transaction history with advanced filtering, sorting, and pagination. [Learn More](https://www.helius.dev/docs/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

[Helius Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=8dc7d328f4e40fdaa0746889c10be474)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=a2ba5e6cf5d5173b0e44b958556367d1)](https://www.helius.dev/)

![CN](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/CN.svg)

简体中文

搜索...

⌘KAsk AI

搜索...

Navigation

Shred Delivery

Shred Delivery

**需要测试版访问**：Shred Delivery目前处于测试阶段，提供白手套配置。访问权限有限，需要Helius团队的批准。请在下方申请测试版访问。

[申请测试版访问\
-------\
\
提交您的Shred Delivery测试版访问申请](https://form.typeform.com/to/aE6sUFRj?typeform-source=t.co)

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/shred-delivery#%E4%BB%80%E4%B9%88%E6%98%AFshred-delivery%EF%BC%9F)

什么是Shred Delivery？
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Shred Delivery是Helius的**通过UDP传输原始Solana分片的专门服务**，旨在为您提供尽早访问Solana原始交易数据的机会。通过直接从网络传输未处理的分片，Shred Delivery为高频交易（HFT）、套利策略和其他对延迟敏感的应用提供了显著的竞争优势。

最早访问
----

接收生成的原始Solana分片，提供对网络活动的最快洞察。

未处理数据
-----

访问原始形式的数据，允许根据您的特定交易策略进行定制处理。

验证者优势
-----

Helius是按质押量排名的顶级验证者，比质押量较少的验证者和未质押的RPC节点更快接收分片。

白手套配置
-----

精心配置的访问确保最佳性能和Helius团队的专属支持。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/shred-delivery#shred-delivery-%E4%B8%8E-laserstream%EF%BC%9A%E5%BF%AB%E9%80%9F%E6%AF%94%E8%BE%83)

Shred Delivery 与 LaserStream：快速比较
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**简而言之**：Shred Delivery 通过直接从网络传递原始、未处理的分片，提供**尽可能早的链上信号**。然而，您必须实现自定义的去分片逻辑来处理这些原始数据。对于具有承诺保证和开发者友好工具的处理数据，请参见 [LaserStream](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/laserstream)
。

| 功能  | Shred Delivery | LaserStream |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **数据类型** | 原始、未处理的分片 | 具有承诺保证的处理数据 |
| **延迟** | **尽可能早** - 在任何处理之前 | 超低延迟的处理数据 |
| **处理** | **您必须处理原始数据** - 需要自定义去分片逻辑 | 开箱即用 - 数据已处理并可直接使用 |
| **最佳用途** | 高频交易、套利（当毫秒至关重要时） | 生产应用、分析、后端服务 |
| **设置** | 高端配置（需要测试版访问） | 开发者友好的 SDK，直接替换 |

[了解 LaserStream\
--------------\
\
了解 LaserStream 如何提供具有承诺保证和可靠性特征的处理数据](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/laserstream)

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/shred-delivery#%E4%BB%80%E4%B9%88%E6%98%AF%E5%88%86%E7%89%87%EF%BC%9F)

什么是分片？
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

在 Solana 中，交易被分解为称为\*\*“分片”\*\*的小数据包，以促进高效和快速的网络传播。每个分片都是交易数据的一个片段，经过优化以适应标准网络包，确保验证者能够快速分发和重建成完整的区块。 这种架构对于维持 Solana 的高吞吐量和低延迟至关重要，而 Shred Delivery 直接接入此原始数据流，在任何处理发生之前。[深入了解：理解 Solana 分片\
-----------------\
\
阅读我们全面的博客文章，解释 Solana 的分片机制如何工作以及为何对交易重要](https://www.helius.dev/blog/solana-shreds)

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/shred-delivery#%E8%AF%A6%E7%BB%86%E6%AF%94%E8%BE%83%EF%BC%9Ashred-delivery-%E4%B8%8E-laserstream)

详细比较：Shred Delivery 与 LaserStream
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

虽然 Shred Delivery 和 LaserStream 都是 Helius 的旗舰数据流产品，但它们的用途不同：

Shred Delivery
--------------

**尽早获取数据**

*   原始分片在生成时即被传送
*   **尽早获取链上信号** - 无处理延迟
*   需要自定义的分片处理逻辑
*   仅限高级定制服务
*   高频交易者和套利策略

LaserStream
-----------

**一站式处理数据**

*   承诺级别的保证（已处理、已确认、已完成）
*   历史重播功能
*   开发者友好的 SDK
*   自动重新连接
*   生产应用和分析

**何时选择：**

*   当您需要**尽早访问**原始交易数据并具备处理原始分片的技术能力时，选择 **Shred Delivery**。Shred Delivery 通过直接从网络传送未处理的分片提供绝对最低的延迟——但您必须实现自己的分片处理逻辑。
*   当您需要可靠的、具有承诺保证的处理数据、历史重播功能和开发者友好的工具时，选择 **LaserStream**。LaserStream 提供具有承诺级别保证的处理交易，非常适合需要可靠数据传输而无需自定义处理基础设施的生产应用。

[LaserStream 文档\
--------------\
\
了解 LaserStream 的可靠性功能处理数据流](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/laserstream)

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/shred-delivery#helius-%E9%AA%8C%E8%AF%81%E8%80%85%E4%BC%98%E5%8A%BF)

Helius 验证者优势
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Helius 是按权益排名的顶级验证者，比权益较少的验证者和无权益的 RPC 节点更快接收分片。在 Turbine 中，具有较高权益权重的验证者在数据传播树中优先接收数据，这意味着区块领导者首先将分片发送给像 Helius 这样的高权益验证者。 这种基于权益的传播确保我们在网络数据流中尽早接收到碎片。虽然其他提供商必须等待二次传播或依赖于无权益的基础设施，但我们的验证者位置使我们能够直接、优先访问流经网络的原始交易数据。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/shred-delivery#%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82)

技术要求
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

为了有效利用碎片传递，您的系统应具备：

碎片重组能力
------

自定义逻辑以从原始碎片重建完整交易

低延迟基础设施
-------

优化为微秒级处理的高性能系统

交易逻辑集成
------

能够在未处理数据上采取行动，并具备适当的风险管理

网络优化
----

优化的网络配置以最小化处理延迟

**需要技术专长**：碎片传递通过UDP提供原始、未处理的碎片。您的团队必须具备处理碎片重组和实施适当处理逻辑的技术能力。

此页面对您有帮助吗？

是否

[上一页](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/data-streaming/quickstart)
[概览下一代 Solana 数据流服务，具备超低延迟、历史回放和多节点可靠性。专为高性能应用而设计。\
\
下一页](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/laserstream)

⌘I

在此页面

[Helius Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=8dc7d328f4e40fdaa0746889c10be474)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=a2ba5e6cf5d5173b0e44b958556367d1)](https://www.helius.dev/)

Shred Delivery

Shred Delivery

**Beta Access Required**: Shred Delivery is currently in beta with white glove provisioning. Access is limited and requires approval from the Helius team. Request beta access below.

[Request Beta Access\
-------------------\
\
Submit your application for Shred Delivery beta access](https://form.typeform.com/to/aE6sUFRj?typeform-source=t.co)

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/shred-delivery#what-is-shred-delivery)

What is Shred Delivery?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Shred Delivery is Helius’s **specialized delivery of raw Solana shreds via UDP**, designed to provide you with the earliest possible access to Solana’s raw transaction data. By delivering unprocessed shreds directly from the network, Shred Delivery offers a significant competitive edge for high-frequency trading (HFT), arbitrage strategies, and other latency-sensitive applications.

Earliest Access
---------------

Receive raw Solana shreds as they are produced, providing the fastest insight into network activity.

Unprocessed Data
----------------

Access data in its raw form, allowing for customized processing tailored to your specific trading strategies.

Validator Advantage
-------------------

Helius is the top validator by stake and receives shreds faster than validators with less stake and non-staked RPC nodes.

White Glove Provisioning
------------------------

Carefully provisioned access ensures optimal performance and dedicated support from the Helius team.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/shred-delivery#shred-delivery-vs-laserstream:-quick-comparison)

Shred Delivery vs. LaserStream: Quick Comparison
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**TL;DR**: Shred Delivery provides the **earliest possible on-chain signal** by delivering raw, unprocessed shreds directly from the network. However, you must implement custom deshredding logic to process this raw data. For processed data with commitment guarantees and developer-friendly tooling, see [LaserStream](https://www.helius.dev/docs/laserstream)
.

| Feature | Shred Delivery | LaserStream |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Data Type** | Raw, unprocessed shreds | Processed data with commitment guarantees |
| **Latency** | **Earliest possible** - before any processing | Ultra-low latency processed data |
| **Processing** | **You must process raw data** - requires custom deshredding logic | Turnkey - data is processed and ready to use |
| **Best For** | High-frequency trading, arbitrage (when milliseconds matter) | Production applications, analytics, backend services |
| **Setup** | White glove provisioning (beta access required) | Developer-friendly SDKs, drop-in replacement |

[Learn About LaserStream\
-----------------------\
\
See how LaserStream delivers processed data with commitment guarantees and reliability features](https://www.helius.dev/docs/laserstream)

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/shred-delivery#what-are-shreds)

What Are Shreds?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In Solana, transactions are broken down into smaller data packets called **“shreds”** to facilitate efficient and rapid propagation across the network. Each shred is a fragment of transaction data, optimized to fit within standard network packets, ensuring swift distribution and reconstruction into complete blocks by validators. This architecture is pivotal for maintaining Solana’s high throughput and low latency, and Shred Delivery taps directly into this raw data stream before any processing occurs.[Deep Dive: Understanding Solana Shreds\
--------------------------------------\
\
Read our comprehensive blog post explaining how Solana’s shred mechanism works and why it matters for trading](https://www.helius.dev/blog/solana-shreds)

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/shred-delivery#detailed-comparison:-shred-delivery-vs-laserstream)

Detailed Comparison: Shred Delivery vs. LaserStream
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While both Shred Delivery and LaserStream are flagship data streaming offerings from Helius, they serve distinct purposes:

Shred Delivery
--------------

**Earliest Possible Data**

*   Raw shreds delivered as they’re produced
*   **Earliest possible on-chain signal** - no processing delay
*   Requires custom deshredding logic
*   White glove provisioning only
*   High-frequency traders & arbitrage strategies

LaserStream
-----------

**Turnkey Processed Data**

*   Commitment-level guarantees (processed, confirmed, finalized)
*   Historical replay capabilities
*   Developer-friendly SDKs
*   Automatic reconnection
*   Production applications & analytics

**When to choose each:**

*   **Choose Shred Delivery** when you need the **earliest possible access** to raw transaction data and have the technical capability to process raw shreds. Shred Delivery provides the absolute lowest latency by delivering unprocessed shreds directly from the network—but you must implement your own deshredding and processing logic.
*   **Choose LaserStream** when you need reliable, processed data with commitment guarantees, historical replay capabilities, and developer-friendly tooling. LaserStream delivers processed transactions with commitment-level guarantees, making it ideal for production applications that need reliable data delivery without custom processing infrastructure.

[LaserStream Documentation\
-------------------------\
\
Learn about LaserStream’s processed data streaming with reliability features](https://www.helius.dev/docs/laserstream)

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/shred-delivery#the-helius-validator-advantage)

The Helius Validator Advantage
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Helius is a top validator by stake and receives shreds faster than validators with less stake and non-staked RPC nodes. In Turbine, validators with higher stake weights receive priority in the data propagation tree, meaning block leaders send shreds to high-stake validators like Helius first. This stake-weighted propagation ensures we receive shreds at the earliest possible moment in the network’s data flow. While other providers must wait for secondary propagation or rely on unstaked infrastructure, our validator position grants direct, prioritized access to the raw transaction data as it flows through the network.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/shred-delivery#technical-requirements)

Technical Requirements
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To effectively utilize Shred Delivery, your system should have:

Deshredding Capability
----------------------

Custom logic to reconstruct complete transactions from raw shreds

Low-Latency Infrastructure
--------------------------

High-performance systems optimized for microsecond-level processing

Trading Logic Integration
-------------------------

Ability to act on unprocessed data with appropriate risk management

Network Optimization
--------------------

Optimized network configuration for minimal processing delays

**Technical Expertise Required**: Shred Delivery provides raw, unprocessed shreds via UDP. Your team must have the technical capability to handle deshredding and implement appropriate processing logic.

质押

使用 Helius SDK 进行编程化 Solana 质押

**零佣金验证器**：使用 Helius 验证器进行质押，享受 0% 佣金率，保留 100% 的质押奖励。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#%E5%BF%AB%E9%80%9F%E6%A6%82%E8%A7%88)

快速概览
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Helius SDK 提供简单的方法以编程方式处理完整的 SOL 质押生命周期。非常适合构建质押界面、DeFi 协议或自动化质押策略。

创建与委托
-----

在一次交易中设置新的质押账户并委托给验证器

监控与管理
-----

跟踪奖励、检查状态并管理现有质押账户

提现与赎回
-----

在冷却期后停用质押并提取 SOL

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#%E5%AE%89%E8%A3%85%E4%B8%8E%E8%AE%BE%E7%BD%AE)

安装与设置
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

npm

yarn

pnpm

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    npm install helius-sdk @solana/web3.js bs58
    

Setup

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    import { Helius } from 'helius-sdk';
    import { Keypair, Transaction } from '@solana/web3.js';
    import bs58 from 'bs58';
    
    // Initialize Helius client
    const helius = new Helius('YOUR_API_KEY');
    
    // Your wallet keypair (load from your secure storage)
    const payer = Keypair.fromSecretKey(/* your secret key */);
    

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#%E8%B4%A8%E6%8A%BC%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80)

质押基础
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Solana 质押如何运作

**质押账户**：一种特殊账户，用于锁定 SOL 并将其委托给验证器。每个质押账户仅指向一个验证器。**奖励**：验证器通过保障网络安全获得奖励。这些奖励分配给所有委托给该验证器的质押账户。**生命周期**：创建 → 委托 → 获得奖励 → 停用 → 提现

为何选择 Helius 验证器

*   **0% 佣金**：保留 100% 的质押奖励
*   **高性能**：可靠的区块生产和最小的停机时间
*   **易于集成**：针对 Helius SDK 优化，内置辅助工具

时间与周期

*   **激活**：质押在下一个周期开始时生效（约 2 天）
*   **停用**：在当前周期结束时生效
*   **冷却**：停用的质押可在周期结束后立即提取

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#%E5%85%A5%E9%97%A8%E6%8C%87%E5%8D%97)

入门指南
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   快速开始
    
*   完整示例
    

仅需三行代码即可质押 SOL：

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    // 1. Create the staking transaction
    const { serializedTx, stakeAccountPubkey } = 
      await helius.rpc.createStakeTransaction(payer.publicKey, 1.5);
    
    // 2. Sign and send
    const tx = Transaction.from(bs58.decode(serializedTx));
    tx.partialSign(payer);
    const signature = await helius.connection.sendRawTransaction(tx.serialize());
    
    console.log(`Staked! Transaction: ${signature}`);
    console.log(`Stake Account: ${stakeAccountPubkey}`);
    

SDK 会自动处理租金计算和质押账户创建。`1.5` 参数是您想要质押的 SOL 数量。

包含错误处理的完整质押实现：

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    async function stakeSOL(amountInSol: number) {
      try {
        // Create staking transaction
        const { serializedTx, stakeAccountPubkey } = 
          await helius.rpc.createStakeTransaction(payer.publicKey, amountInSol);
        
        // Deserialize and sign transaction
        const transaction = Transaction.from(bs58.decode(serializedTx));
        transaction.partialSign(payer);
        
        // Send transaction
        const signature = await helius.connection.sendRawTransaction(
          transaction.serialize(),
          { 
            skipPreflight: false,
            preflightCommitment: 'confirmed'
          }
        );
        
        // Wait for confirmation
        await helius.connection.confirmTransaction(signature, 'confirmed');
        
        return {
          signature,
          stakeAccount: stakeAccountPubkey,
          amount: amountInSol
        };
        
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Staking failed:', error);
        throw error;
      }
    }
    
    // Usage
    const result = await stakeSOL(2.5);
    console.log(`Successfully staked ${result.amount} SOL`);
    

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#sdk-%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%E5%8F%82%E8%80%83)

SDK 方法参考
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

createStakeTransaction(owner, amount)

创建一个可以签名和发送的完整质押交易。**参数：**

*   `owner` (PublicKey): 将拥有质押账户的钱包
*   `amount` (number): 要质押的 SOL 数量

**返回：**

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    {
      serializedTx: string,        // Base58 encoded transaction
      stakeAccountPubkey: string   // New stake account address
    }
    

**示例：**

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    const result = await helius.rpc.createStakeTransaction(
      payer.publicKey, 
      1.5  // 1.5 SOL
    );
getStakeInstructions(owner, amount)

返回质押指令（对于自定义交易构建很有用）。**返回：**

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    {
      instructions: TransactionInstruction[],
      stakeAccount: Keypair
    }
    

**示例：**

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    const { instructions } = await helius.rpc.getStakeInstructions(
      payer.publicKey, 
      1.5
    );
    
    // Use with Smart Transactions
    const signature = await helius.rpc.sendSmartTransaction(
      instructions, 
      [payer]
    );
getHeliusStakeAccounts(wallet)

检索委托给 Helius 验证器的钱包的所有质押账户。**示例：**

报告错误代码

复制

    const accounts = await helius.rpc.getHeliusStakeAccounts(
      payer.publicKey.toBase58()
    );
    
    accounts.forEach(account => {
      const delegation = account.account.data.parsed.info.stake.delegation;
      console.log(`Account: ${account.pubkey}`);
      console.log(`Stake: ${delegation.stake / LAMPORTS_PER_SOL} SOL`);
    });
createUnstakeTransaction(owner, stakeAccount)

创建一个交易以停用（开始取消质押）质押账户。**示例：**

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    const tx = await helius.rpc.createUnstakeTransaction(
      payer.publicKey,
      stakeAccountPubkey
    );
    
    const transaction = Transaction.from(bs58.decode(tx));
    transaction.partialSign(payer);
    await helius.connection.sendRawTransaction(transaction.serialize());
getWithdrawableAmount(stakeAccount, includeRent?)

检查可以从已停用的质押账户中提取多少 SOL。**参数：**

*   `includeRent` (boolean): 是否包括免租金额

**示例：**

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    const available = await helius.rpc.getWithdrawableAmount(stakeAccountPubkey);
    const total = await helius.rpc.getWithdrawableAmount(stakeAccountPubkey, true);
    
    console.log(`Available now: ${available / LAMPORTS_PER_SOL} SOL`);
    console.log(`Total balance: ${total / LAMPORTS_PER_SOL} SOL`);
createWithdrawTransaction(owner, stakeAccount, destination, amount)

    const tx = await helius.rpc.createWithdrawTransaction(
      payer.publicKey,
      stakeAccountPubkey,
      destinationPubkey,
      withdrawAmount  // in lamports
    );

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#%E5%AE%8C%E6%95%B4%E8%B4%A8%E6%8A%BC%E5%B7%A5%E4%BD%9C%E6%B5%81%E7%A8%8B)

完整质押工作流程
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

创建和委托

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    // Stake 2 SOL to Helius validator
    const { serializedTx, stakeAccountPubkey } = 
      await helius.rpc.createStakeTransaction(payer.publicKey, 2.0);
    
    const tx = Transaction.from(bs58.decode(serializedTx));
    tx.partialSign(payer);
    
    const signature = await helius.connection.sendRawTransaction(tx.serialize());
    console.log(`Stake created: ${stakeAccountPubkey}`);
    

2

监控您的质押

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    // Get all your Helius stake accounts
    const accounts = await helius.rpc.getHeliusStakeAccounts(
      payer.publicKey.toBase58()
    );
    
    console.log(`You have ${accounts.length} active stake accounts`);
    
    accounts.forEach((account, index) => {
      const info = account.account.data.parsed.info;
      const delegation = info.stake.delegation;
      
      console.log(`Stake ${index + 1}:`);
      console.log(`  Amount: ${delegation.stake / LAMPORTS_PER_SOL} SOL`);
      console.log(`  Activated: Epoch ${delegation.activationEpoch}`);
      console.log(`  Status: ${info.meta.lockup.unixTimestamp === 0 ? 'Active' : 'Locked'}`);
    });
    

3

停用（开始解除质押）

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    // Begin the unstaking process
    const unstakeTx = await helius.rpc.createUnstakeTransaction(
      payer.publicKey,
      stakeAccountPubkey
    );
    
    const tx = Transaction.from(bs58.decode(unstakeTx));
    tx.partialSign(payer);
    
    await helius.connection.sendRawTransaction(tx.serialize());
    console.log('Deactivation started. Will be withdrawable next epoch.');
    

4

提取 SOL

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    // Check withdrawable amount
    const withdrawable = await helius.rpc.getWithdrawableAmount(
      stakeAccountPubkey, 
      true  // include rent
    );
    
    if (withdrawable > 0) {
      // Create withdrawal instruction
      const withdrawInstruction = helius.rpc.getWithdrawInstruction(
        payer.publicKey,
        stakeAccountPubkey,
        payer.publicKey,  // withdraw to same wallet
        withdrawable
      );
      
      // Send using Smart Transactions for better reliability
      const signature = await helius.rpc.sendSmartTransaction(
        [withdrawInstruction], 
        [payer]
      );
      
      console.log(`Withdrawn ${withdrawable / LAMPORTS_PER_SOL} SOL`);
    }
    

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#%E9%AB%98%E7%BA%A7%E6%A8%A1%E5%BC%8F)

高级模式
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   浏览器集成
    
*   批量操作
    
*   智能交易
    

对于使用钱包适配器的浏览器应用程序：

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    // Get instructions instead of full transaction
    const { instructions, stakeAccount } = await helius.rpc.getStakeInstructions(
      wallet.publicKey,
      stakeAmount
    );
    
    // Let the wallet handle transaction building and signing
    const transaction = new Transaction().add(...instructions);
    
    // Sign with wallet adapter
    const signature = await wallet.sendTransaction(transaction, connection);
    
    console.log(`Stake account: ${stakeAccount.publicKey.toBase58()}`);
    

高效地为多个钱包进行质押：

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    async function batchStake(wallets: Keypair[], amount: number) {
      const promises = wallets.map(async (wallet) => {
        try {
          const { serializedTx, stakeAccountPubkey } = 
            await helius.rpc.createStakeTransaction(wallet.publicKey, amount);
          
          const tx = Transaction.from(bs58.decode(serializedTx));
          tx.partialSign(wallet);
          
          return helius.connection.sendRawTransaction(tx.serialize());
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(`Failed to stake for ${wallet.publicKey.toBase58()}:`, error);
          return null;
        }
      });
      
      const results = await Promise.allSettled(promises);
      const successful = results.filter(r => r.status === 'fulfilled').length;
      
      console.log(`Successfully staked for ${successful}/${wallets.length} wallets`);
    }
    

使用智能交易以提高可靠性和优化：

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    // Get individual instructions
    const { instructions } = await helius.rpc.getStakeInstructions(
      payer.publicKey,
      2.5
    );
    
    // Send with Smart Transaction features:
    // - Automatic priority fee optimization
    // - Retry logic with backoff
    // - Better error handling
    const signature = await helius.rpc.sendSmartTransaction(
      instructions,
      [payer],
      {
        skipPreflight: false,
        maxRetries: 3
      }
    );
    
    console.log(`Smart transaction sent: ${signature}`);
    

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#%E9%87%8D%E8%A6%81%E6%8F%90%E7%A4%BA)

重要提示
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Epoch 时间**：Solana 的 epoch 大约持续 2 天。质押在下一个 epoch 开始时激活，停用在当前 epoch 结束时生效。

**租金考虑**：质押账户需要租金豁免储备（约 0.00228 SOL）。提取全部余额将关闭账户。

**硬件钱包**：用户将看到两个签名提示 - 一个用于质押账户（预签名），另一个用于费用支付者。请相应设计您的用户体验。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#%E5%BF%AB%E9%80%9F%E5%8F%82%E8%80%83)

快速参考
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

需要快速提醒吗？以下是基本方法：

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    // Stake SOL
    await helius.rpc.createStakeTransaction(owner, amountInSol);
    
    // Check your stakes  
    await helius.rpc.getHeliusStakeAccounts(ownerAddress);
    
    // Start unstaking
    await helius.rpc.createUnstakeTransaction(owner, stakeAccount);
    
    // Check withdrawable amount
    await helius.rpc.getWithdrawableAmount(stakeAccount, includeRent);
    
    // Withdraw SOL
    helius.rpc.getWithdrawInstruction(owner, stakeAccount, destination, amount);
    

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/staking/how-to-stake-with-helius-programmatically#%E4%B8%8B%E4%B8%80%E6%AD%A5)

[Helius Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=8dc7d328f4e40fdaa0746889c10be474)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=a2ba5e6cf5d5173b0e44b958556367d1)](https://www.helius.dev/)

Navigation

Webhooks

Solana Webhooks: Real-Time Blockchain Event Notifications

Helius Webhooks enable seamless monitoring of Solana on-chain events, such as sales, listings, swaps, and more. We offer a user-friendly interface, programmatic API, and SDK access for easily creating and managing webhooks. For frequently asked questions about webhooks, please refer to our [Webhooks FAQ](https://www.helius.dev/docs/faqs/webhooks)
.

Helius may retry webhook deliveries if your server does not respond successfully, and you might receive duplicate events. For details on retries and handling duplicates, see the [Webhooks FAQ](https://www.helius.dev/docs/faqs/webhooks#retries)
.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks#pricing)

Pricing
------------------------------------------------------------

Webhook events are charged at **1 credit** when Helius processes and sends the event to your endpoint. You are charged regardless of whether your endpoint successfully processes the webhook or not. Editing, adding, or deleting a webhook via the API will cost 100 credits/request.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks#types-of-webhooks)

Types of Webhooks
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We currently offer several types of webhooks tailored to different needs:

*   **Enhanced Transaction Webhooks**: Provide human-readable, parsed data for specific transaction types (e.g., NFT sales) related to the addresses you monitor. This is ideal if you want filtered, actionable insights.
*   **Raw Transaction Webhooks**: This option delivers raw transaction data for all transactions involving the addresses you monitor. It does not allow filtering by transaction type.
*   **Discord Webhooks**: Stream updates for specific transaction types directly to a designated Discord channel as formatted messages. To use this option, you must submit your Discord Webhook URL.

Raw Transaction Webhooks offer lower latency since they do not involve parsing event types.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks#event-payload-example)

Event Payload Example

Enhanced

Report incorrect code

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks#quick-start)

Quick Start
--------------------------------------------------------------------

We provide three convenient methods to create, edit, and manage webhooks on Helius.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks#via-helius-dashboard)

Via Helius Dashboard

The Helius UI is perfect if you prefer a no-code solution with additional features like viewing logs and sending test webhook events. You can access it directly through our [Dashboard](https://dashboard.helius.dev/webhooks)
. You can add up to 25 addresses via the Dashboard. To monitor more than 25 addresses, you can use our API or SDK.

Via Dashboard

You can create a webhook directly from the dashboard:

1.  Navigate to the [Helius Dashboard](https://dashboard.helius.dev/webhooks)
    
2.  Click “Add Webhook”
3.  Complete the required fields
4.  Click “Create Webhook”

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks#via-helius-api)

Via Helius API

If you’re not working with Typescript or Javascript, you’ll need to interact with our webhooks through REST API:[API Reference\
-------------\
\
Learn about the Webhooks API endpoints and how to use them.](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/webhooks)

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks#via-helius-sdk)

Via Helius SDK

The easiest—and most enjoyable—way to interact with Helius webhooks is through our official SDKs. We currently offer SDKs for **TypeScript** and **Rust**.

[TypeScript SDK\
--------------\
\
The TypeScript SDK provides powerful abstractions for webhooks.](https://github.com/helius-labs/helius-sdk#webhooks)
[Rust SDK\
--------\
\
Our Rust SDK offers native Rust support for Helius webhooks.](https://github.com/helius-labs/helius-rust-sdk)

The SDKs provide powerful abstractions that enhance the functionality of webhooks.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks#example-uses)

Example Uses
----------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Bots**
    *   When an NFT is listed on marketplace X, trigger an “NFT buy” action.
    *   When a margin position is unhealthy, trigger a “liquidation” action.
*   **Monitoring & Alerts**
    *   When a program emits a certain log, it triggers PagerDuty integration.
    *   When a token account balance changes by more than X%, use Dialect to communicate a warning action.
*   **Event-driven Indexing**
    *   When any transaction occurs for a given program, send it directly to your database or backend.
*   **Notifications & Activity Tracking**
    *   When transferring from wallet X to wallet Y — send a Slack notification or email.
*   **Analytics & Logs**
    *   When event X happens, send it to an ETL pipeline or persist it directly on Helius to view trends over time.
*   **Workflow Automation**
    *   When event X happens, trigger any set of actions.

简体中文

搜索...

⌘KAsk AI

搜索...

Navigation

Webhook

Solana Webhooks：实时区块链事件通知

Helius Webhooks 使监控 Solana 链上事件（如销售、上架、交换等）变得无缝便捷。我们提供用户友好的界面、可编程的 API 和 SDK 访问，轻松创建和管理 Webhooks。 有关 Webhooks 的常见问题，请参阅我们的 [Webhooks 常见问题解答](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/faqs/webhooks)
。

如果您的服务器未成功响应，Helius 可能会重试 webhook 传递，您可能会收到重复的事件。有关重试和处理重复的详细信息，请参阅 [Webhooks FAQ](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/faqs/webhooks#retries)
。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/webhooks#%E5%AE%9A%E4%BB%B7)

定价
---------------------------------------------------------------------

当 Helius 处理并将事件发送到您的端点时，webhook 事件将收取 **1 个信用**。无论您的端点是否成功处理 webhook，您都将被收费。通过 API 编辑、添加或删除 webhook 将花费 100 个信用/请求。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/webhooks#webhooks-%E7%B1%BB%E5%9E%8B)

Webhooks 类型
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

我们目前提供几种针对不同需求定制的 webhooks 类型：

*   **增强型交易 Webhooks**：提供特定交易类型（例如，NFT 销售）的可读解析数据，适用于您监控的地址。如果您需要过滤的、可操作的见解，这是理想的选择。
*   **原始交易 Webhooks**：此选项提供涉及您监控地址的所有交易的原始交易数据。它不允许按交易类型进行过滤。
*   **Discord Webhooks**：将特定交易类型的更新直接流式传输到指定的 Discord 频道，作为格式化消息。要使用此选项，您必须提交您的 Discord Webhook URL。

原始交易 Webhooks 提供较低的延迟，因为它们不涉及事件类型的解析。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/webhooks#%E4%BA%8B%E4%BB%B6%E8%B4%9F%E8%BD%BD%E7%A4%BA%E4%BE%8B)

事件负载示例

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/webhooks#%E5%BF%AB%E9%80%9F%E5%BC%80%E5%A7%8B)

快速开始
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

我们提供三种便捷的方法来创建、编辑和管理 Helius 上的 webhooks。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/webhooks#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87-helius-%E4%BB%AA%E8%A1%A8%E6%9D%BF)

通过 Helius 仪表板

如果您更喜欢无代码解决方案，并希望使用查看日志和发送测试 webhook 事件等附加功能，Helius UI 是完美的选择。您可以直接通过我们的 [仪表板](https://dashboard.helius.dev/webhooks)
 访问它。您可以通过仪表板添加最多 25 个地址。要监控超过 25 个地址，您可以使用我们的 API 或 SDK。

通过仪表板

您可以直接从仪表板创建一个 webhook：

1.  导航到 [Helius 仪表板](https://dashboard.helius.dev/webhooks)
    
2.  点击 “添加 Webhook”
3.  完成必填字段
4.  点击 “创建 Webhook”

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/webhooks#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87-helius-api)

通过 Helius API

如果您不使用 Typescript 或 Javascript，您需要通过 REST API 与我们的 webhooks 交互：[API 参考\
------\
\
了解 Webhooks API 端点及其使用方法。](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/webhooks)

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/webhooks#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87-helius-sdk)

通过 Helius SDK

与 Helius webhooks 交互的最简单且最愉快的方式是通过我们的官方 SDK。我们目前提供 **TypeScript** 和 **Rust** 的 SDK。

[TypeScript SDK\
--------------\
\
TypeScript SDK 为 webhooks 提供强大的抽象。](https://github.com/helius-labs/helius-sdk#webhooks)
[Rust SDK\
--------\
\
我们的 Rust SDK 为 Helius webhooks 提供原生 Rust 支持。](https://github.com/helius-labs/helius-rust-sdk)

SDK 提供强大的抽象，增强了 webhooks 的功能。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/webhooks#%E7%A4%BA%E4%BE%8B%E7%94%A8%E9%80%94)

示例用途
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **机器人**
    *   当 NFT 在市场 X 上架时，触发 “NFT 购买” 动作。
    *   当保证金头寸不健康时，触发 “清算” 动作。
*   **监控与警报**
    *   当程序发出某个日志时，触发 PagerDuty 集成。
    *   当代币账户余额变化超过 X% 时，使用 Dialect 传达警告动作。
*   **事件驱动的索引**
    *   当给定程序发生任何交易时，直接将其发送到您的数据库或后端。
*   **通知与活动跟踪**
    *   从钱包 X 转移到钱包 Y 时，发送 Slack 通知或电子邮件。
*   **分析与日志**
    *   当事件 X 发生时，将其发送到 ETL 管道或直接在 Helius 上持久化以查看长期趋势。
*   **工作流自动化**
    *   当事件 X 发生时，触发任何一组动作。

此页面对您有帮助吗？

是否

Understanding Transaction Types
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Transaction types represent different blockchain actions decoded by our system. Each transaction type corresponds to specific on-chain activities like NFT minting, bidding, or staking. Below is the full list of transaction types supported:

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks/transaction-types#mapping-transaction-types-to-sources)

Mapping Transaction Types to Sources
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each transaction type is generated by specific program sources. Understanding these relationships helps identify which programs are triggering particular transaction types. The mappings below illustrate the relationship between sources (programs) and specific transaction types:

*   **Type-to-Source**: Shows which programs generate a specific transaction type
*   **Source-to-Type**: Shows all transaction types a specific program can generate

For example, **NFT\_GLOBAL\_BID** transactions are generated by **MAGIC\_EDEN** or **SOLANART**, while **CANDY\_MACHINE\_V2** exclusively generates **NFT\_MINT** events.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/webhooks/transaction-types#type-to-source-reference)

Type-to-Source Reference
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This mapping shows which program sources can generate each transaction type.

Using Transaction Types in Your Code
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When implementing webhook listeners, you can filter for specific transaction types of interest. Here’s a simple example of how to listen for NFT sale events:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    // Example webhook handler for NFT sales
    app.post('/webhook', (req, res) => {
      const event = req.body;
      
      // Filter for NFT sale transactions
      if (event.type === 'NFT_SALE') {
        console.log('NFT Sale detected!');
        console.log('Seller:', event.seller);
        console.log('Buyer:', event.buyer);
        console.log('Price:', event.amount);
        console.log('NFT:', event.nft?.mint);
        
        // Process the sale event
        // ...
      }
      
      res.status(200).send('OK');
    });
    

You can use the Type-to-Source and Source-to-Type mappings to anticipate which programs will generate specific transaction types.

Solana Webhook 交易类型

理解交易类型
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

交易类型代表我们系统解码的不同区块链操作。每种交易类型对应特定的链上活动，如 NFT 铸造、竞标或质押。 以下是支持的交易类型的完整列表：

将交易类型映射到来源
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

每种交易类型由特定的程序来源生成。理解这些关系有助于识别哪些程序正在触发特定的交易类型。 下面的映射展示了来源（程序）与特定交易类型之间的关系：

*   **类型到来源**：显示哪些程序生成特定的交易类型
*   **来源到类型**：显示特定程序可以生成的所有交易类型

例如，**NFT\_GLOBAL\_BID** 交易由 **MAGIC\_EDEN** 或 **SOLANART** 生成，而 **CANDY\_MACHINE\_V2** 专门生成 **NFT\_MINT** 事件。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/webhooks/transaction-types#%E7%B1%BB%E5%9E%8B%E5%88%B0%E6%9D%A5%E6%BA%90%E5%8F%82%E8%80%83)

类型到来源参考
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

此映射显示哪些程序来源可以生成每种交易类型。

Using Transaction Types in Your Code
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When implementing webhook listeners, you can filter for specific transaction types of interest. Here’s a simple example of how to listen for NFT sale events:

报告错误代码

复制

询问AI

    
    javascript
    // 用于 NFT 销售的示例 webhook 处理程序
    app.post('/webhook', (req, res) => {
      const event = req.body;
      
      // 过滤 NFT 销售交易
      if (event.type === 'NFT_SALE') {
        console.log('检测到 NFT 销售！');
        console.log('卖家:', event.seller);
        console.log('买家:', event.buyer);
        console.log('价格:', event.amount);
        console.log('NFT:', event.nft?.mint);
        
        // 处理销售事件
        // ...
      }
      
      res.status(200).send('OK');
    });
    

您可以使用 Type-to-Source 和 Source-to-Type 映射来预测哪些程序将生成特定的交易类型。

Navigation

Compression

What is ZK Compression on Solana?

[ZK Compression](https://www.zkcompression.com/)
 is a generalized compression framework that allows developers to store data on Solana at a fraction of the cost. After helping develop cNFT compression, Helius saw the need to build a generalized system. So, along with the [Light team](https://lightprotocol.com/)
, we built ZK Compression to allow developers to store arbitrary data in _compressed accounts_, akin to native Solana accounts.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zk-compression/introduction#photon:-the-zk-compression-indexer)

Photon: the ZK Compression Indexer
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Helius built [Photon](https://github.com/helius-labs/photon)
, the ZK Compression indexer. In ZK Compression, programs log compressed account data in Solana transactions and store the fingerprint of that data in validator memory. Photon indexes Solana transactions to parse and store compressed account data. It then exposes a [ZK Compression](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/zk-compression)
 API similar to Solana’s native API to help users access compression data. Though developers can directly host Photon, we expose a Photon API to streamline the developer experience.

Please visit the official [ZK Compression docs](https://www.zkcompression.com/)
 to learn more about ZK Compression and Photon.

# 什么是 Solana 上的 ZK 压缩？ - Helius Docs

Navigation

压缩

什么是 Solana 上的 ZK 压缩？

[ZK 压缩](https://www.zkcompression.com/)
 是一个通用的压缩框架，允许开发者以极低的成本在 Solana 上存储数据。在帮助开发 cNFT 压缩后，Helius 发现需要构建一个通用系统。因此，我们与 [Light 团队](https://lightprotocol.com/)
 一起构建了 ZK 压缩，以允许开发者在 _压缩账户_ 中存储任意数据，类似于 Solana 原生账户。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/zk-compression/introduction#photon%EF%BC%9Azk-%E5%8E%8B%E7%BC%A9%E7%B4%A2%E5%BC%95%E5%99%A8)

Photon：ZK 压缩索引器
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Helius 构建了 [Photon](https://github.com/helius-labs/photon)
，即 ZK Compression 索引器。在 ZK Compression 中，程序在 Solana 交易中记录压缩的账户数据，并将该数据的指纹存储在验证器内存中。Photon 索引 Solana 交易以解析和存储压缩的账户数据。然后，它提供一个类似于 Solana 原生 API 的 [ZK Compression](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/zk-compression)
 API，帮助用户访问压缩数据。虽然开发者可以直接托管 Photon，但我们提供了一个 Photon API 以简化开发者体验。

请访问官方 [ZK 压缩文档](https://www.zkcompression.com/)
 以了解有关 ZK 压缩和 Photon 的更多信息。

此页面对您有帮助吗？

是否

[概述使用 ZK 压缩进行经济高效的 Solana 代币空投。通过 Helius AirShip 的开源分发工具，将空投成本降低 95%。\
\
下一页](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/airship/overview)

使用 Helius 构建您的第一个 Solana 应用

准备好在 Solana 上构建了吗？本指南将引导您使用 Helius API 创建您的第一个应用。您将学习如何获取 NFT 数据、理解响应结构，并了解如何利用我们的基础设施轻松构建强大的应用程序。

1

创建您的免费 Helius 账户
----------------

首先在 [Helius Dashboard](https://dashboard.helius.dev/dashboard)
 创建您的免费账户。您的免费套餐每月包含 100,000 次 DAS API 调用，非常适合入门和构建原型。

2

获取您的 API 密钥
-----------

前往 [API Keys](https://dashboard.helius.dev/api-keys)
 部分并复制您的密钥。此密钥可让您访问所有 Helius API，包括 RPC 节点、DAS API 和增强的交易数据。

3

进行您的第一次 API 调用
--------------

让我们从一个实际示例开始：从钱包中获取 NFT。我们将使用 [getAssetsByOwner](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/das/getassetsbyowner)
 方法查询 `86xCn…o2MMY`（Solana 联合创始人 Anatoly Yakovenko 的钱包）拥有的资产。**这里发生了什么？** DAS API 允许您通过一次调用查询压缩和标准 NFT。请注意，响应中包含元数据、图片 URL 和所有权信息——构建丰富用户体验所需的所有数据。

4

理解响应
----

太棒了！您已成功获取 NFT 数据。响应包括：

*   **资产 ID**：每个 NFT 的唯一标识符
*   **元数据**：名称、符号、描述和属性
*   **内容**：图片 URL 和文件信息
*   **所有权**：当前所有者和权限信息

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/quickstart#%E7%94%A8%E4%BB%A3%E7%A0%81%E6%9E%84%E5%BB%BA)

用代码构建
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

现在让我们在实际应用中实现这一点。我们将创建一个简单的 NFT 投资组合查看器，您可以在此基础上进行扩展。

我们将在此示例中使用 Node.js。请确保您已从 [nodejs.org](https://nodejs.org/en/download)
 安装它。

1

### 设置您的项目

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    mkdir solana-nft-viewer
    cd solana-nft-viewer
    npm init -y
    npm install node-fetch
    

2

### 创建 NFT 投资组合查看器

nft-portfolio.js

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    const fetch = require('node-fetch');
    
    class NFTPortfolioViewer {
      constructor(apiKey) {
        this.apiKey = apiKey;
        this.baseUrl = 'https://mainnet.helius-rpc.com';
      }
    
      async fetchNFTsByOwner(ownerAddress, limit = 10) {
        try {
          const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/?api-key=${this.apiKey}`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
              'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
              jsonrpc: '2.0',
              id: '1',
              method: 'getAssetsByOwner',
              params: {
                ownerAddress,
                page: 1,
                limit,
                displayOptions: {
                  showFungible: false,
                  showNativeBalance: false,
                },
              },
            }),
          });
    
          const data = await response.json();
    
          if (data.error) {
            throw new Error(data.error.message);
          }
    
          return data.result;
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Error fetching NFTs:', error.message);
          throw error;
        }
      }
    
      displayNFTPortfolio(nfts) {
        console.log('\n🖼️  NFT Portfolio Summary');
        console.log('========================');
        console.log(`Total NFTs: ${nfts.total}`);
        console.log(`Showing: ${nfts.items.length} items\n`);
    
        nfts.items.forEach((nft, index) => {
          console.log(`${index + 1}. ${nft.content?.metadata?.name || 'Unnamed NFT'}`);
          console.log(`   Collection: ${nft.grouping?.[0]?.group_value || 'Individual'}`);
          console.log(`   Compressed: ${nft.compression?.compressed ? 'Yes' : 'No'}`);
          console.log(`   Image: ${nft.content?.files?.[0]?.uri || 'No image'}`);
          console.log(`   ID: ${nft.id}\n`);
        });
      }
    
      async getRandomNFT(ownerAddress) {
        const portfolio = await this.fetchNFTsByOwner(ownerAddress, 50);
        
        if (portfolio.items.length === 0) {
          console.log('No NFTs found for this address.');
          return null;
        }
    
        const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * portfolio.items.length);
        return portfolio.items[randomIndex];
      }
    }
    
    // Usage example
    async function main() {
      const viewer = new NFTPortfolioViewer('YOUR_API_KEY');
      
      // Anatoly's wallet address
      const walletAddress = '86xCnPeV69n6t3DnyGvkKobf9FdN2H9oiVDdaMpo2MMY';
      
      console.log('🚀 Fetching NFT portfolio...');
      
      try {
        // Get full portfolio overview
        const portfolio = await viewer.fetchNFTsByOwner(walletAddress);
        viewer.displayNFTPortfolio(portfolio);
        
        // Get a random NFT for featured display
        console.log('🎲 Featured Random NFT:');
        console.log('=====================');
        const randomNFT = await viewer.getRandomNFT(walletAddress);
        
        if (randomNFT) {
          console.log(`Name: ${randomNFT.content?.metadata?.name}`);
          console.log(`Description: ${randomNFT.content?.metadata?.description || 'No description'}`);
          console.log(`Image: ${randomNFT.content?.files?.[0]?.uri}`);
        }
        
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Failed to fetch NFT data:', error.message);
      }
    }
    
    main();
    

3

### 添加您的 API 密钥

将 `YOUR_API_KEY` 替换为您从 Helius 仪表板获取的实际 API 密钥。

4

### 运行您的 NFT 投资组合查看器

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    node nft-portfolio.js
    

5

### 成功！🎉

您已经构建了您的第一个 Solana 应用程序！输出显示：

*   钱包中的 NFT 总数
*   包括压缩状态在内的单个 NFT 详细信息
*   集合信息
*   一个随机精选的 NFT

**您学到了什么：**

*   如何构建对 Helius 的 API 调用
*   处理 DAS API 响应格式
*   处理压缩和标准 NFT
*   为 NFT 操作构建可重用代码

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/quickstart#%E6%9B%B4%E8%BF%9B%E4%B8%80%E6%AD%A5)

# How to Swap Solana Tokens on Orb - Helius Docs

[Skip to main content](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/swap-tokens#content-area)

[Helius Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=8dc7d328f4e40fdaa0746889c10be474)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=a2ba5e6cf5d5173b0e44b958556367d1)](https://www.helius.dev/)

Navigation

Using Orb

How to Swap Solana Tokens on Orb

Block explorers like [Orb](https://orb.helius.dev/)
 are great tools for [finding top Solana coins](https://www.helius.dev/orb/explore-markets)
, researching projects, and deciding whether to buy or sell tokens. To make this process even easier, we’ve added a “Buy” button to every Solana token page indexed on the Orb explorer. All you need to do is connect your wallet and click “Buy” to swap into or out of any SPL token on Solana. This tutorial explains how to swap tokens on Solana using Orb, along with keyboard shortcuts for faster research and easier buys.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/swap-tokens#swapping-solana-tokens-on-orb)

**Swapping Solana Tokens on Orb**
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here is a step-by-step tutorial on finding and trading tokens on Orb.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/swap-tokens#find-the-token)

**Find the Token**

First, find the token you’re looking to swap by either searching by name in Orb’s search bar or by entering the token’s mint address.

![Find Zec Token On Solana Using The Orb Explorer Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/find-zec-token-on-solana-using-the-orb-explorer.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=259d415a6e2f1fe6e8a92e7da83a8a91)

Orb token search bar showing the ZEC token on Solana

For more details, learn about [looking up Solana tokens](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-tokens)
 and [finding SPL mint addresses](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-authorities)
.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/swap-tokens#click-%E2%80%9Cbuy%E2%80%9D)

Click “Buy”

At the top of the page, next to the token’s image and name, click the orange “Buy” button. You will also see key token metrics, including supply, market cap, liquidity, fully diluted value (FDV), current price, holders (on Solana), and 24-hour volume.

![Zec Token Explorer And Swap Button On Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/mxJR5cR2qBt5r4qx/images/zec-token-explorer-and-swap-button-on-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=mxJR5cR2qBt5r4qx&q=85&s=972d5d64fd3fc39c2517364b18fbc250)

Solana token page on the Orb explorer with the “Buy” button highlighted

For this example, we’ll swap SOL for ZEC (Zcash) on Solana.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/swap-tokens#connect-your-wallet)

Connect Your Wallet

Clicking the “Buy” button or pressing the keyboard shortcut “B” opens a dialogue box prompting you to connect your wallet.

![Connect Solana Wallet To The Orb Explorer To Swap Tokens Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/connect-solana-wallet-to-the-orb-explorer-to-swap-tokens.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=c38f6b98591202678c9f4ba46b8a5741)

Dialogue box to connect your wallet, powered by reown

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/swap-tokens#use-the-swap-widget)

Use the Swap Widget

Once connected, you’ll see the main swap widget.

![The Orb Explorer Swap Widget For Trading Tokens On Solana Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/the-orb-explorer-swap-widget-for-trading-tokens-on-solana.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=930d328621c36e454e22a1f6094b9bde)

Orb swap widget indicating a 0.015 SOL swap for ZEC

This swap widget UI lets you choose the asset and amount you want to buy/sell.  Once you click “Buy ZEC,” your wallet will display a confirmation message.

![Phantom Wallet Swap Confirmation For Trading On The Orb Explorer Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/phantom-wallet-swap-confirmation-for-trading-on-the-orb-explorer.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=1822ae7fa7a20cda50125330c2975626)

Phantom swap confirmation message for trading on Orb

Once you click confirm, your trade will be routed through [DFlow’s](https://dflow.net/)
 meta aggregator or Jupiter. DFlow’s intelligent transaction execution stack offers traders the best prices and tightest spreads.

A 0.1% swap fee is applied to all swaps made through the Orb UI.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/swap-tokens#view-swap-details)

View Swap Details

Once the swap is completed, you’ll see a swap confirmation message and a link to [view the transaction details](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-transactions)
. Click this link to see a summary of your trade.

![Sol Zec Swap Transaction Explorer Summary On The Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/sol-zec-swap-transaction-explorer-summary-on-the-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=20bc6788a2e834da2dcff7e05cb60323)

Swap transaction summary page on the Orb explorer

That’s it!  You’ve successfully swapped Solana for ZEC on Orb. To [view your wallet balances](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-wallets)
, go to your wallet page on Orb and click the **Tokens** tab.

![Solana Wallet Explorer Tab On Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/solana-wallet-explorer-tab-on-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=e3e43c855513475c69621c1085b1a779)

Explore token balances for any wallet on Orb

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/swap-tokens#conclusion)

**Conclusion**
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Discovering, researching, and buying tokens on Solana doesn’t need to be a complicated process involving multiple different websites and research tools. The [Orb block explorer](https://orb.helius.dev/)
 provides everything investors need to find, analyze, and buy crypto. For more information, read our other guides on:

*   [Finding Solana Mint Addresses](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-mint-addresses)
    
*   [Researching Solana Token Authorities](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-authorities)
    
*   [Discovering Trending Solana Tokens](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets)

Using Orb

How to Find Top Solana Coins on Orb

The [Orb block explorer](https://orb.helius.dev/)
 has a **Markets** page that highlights the [top coins on Solana](https://orb.helius.dev/markets)
 so you can quickly find the best projects across majors, currencies, DeFi, DePIN, and memecoins. This tutorial explains how to discover tokens on Solana with Orb, use keyboard shortcuts to speed up research, and buy tokens directly through Orb.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets#top-coins-on-solana)

**Top Coins on Solana**
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Markets** page lists the top coins on Solana. Click each tab to view a curated list of assets or use the following numbered keyboard shortcuts:

1.  Trending 
2.  Majors 
3.  DeFi 
4.  Stocks 
5.  Currencies 
6.  DePIN 
7.  Cults

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets#trending-coins)

Trending Coins

The trending tokens tab filters the top coins on Solana by trading volume, minimum market cap, and FDV. To navigate the token list, use the following keyboard shortcuts:

*   Press “W” or ”S” to navigate up and down rows
*   Press “A” or “D” to navigate to the next and previous pages
*   Press “B” to buy the selected token

![Trending Solana Token Explorer Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/mxJR5cR2qBt5r4qx/images/trending-solana-token-explorer-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=mxJR5cR2qBt5r4qx&q=85&s=d64cd7faa780e0383f5cd11a83dc6cea)

Top trending coins tradeable on Solana

If you want to learn more, click the asset’s name to view its [token details page](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-tokens)
.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets#major-assets)

Major Assets

Majors are verified tokens on Solana of reputable, blue-chip assets such as wrapped Bitcoin (BTC), Ethereum (ETH), Hyperliquid (HYPE), Zcash (ZEC), and Monad (MON).

![Explore Top Major Assets On Solana Using The Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/explore-top-major-assets-on-solana-using-the-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=2c2ba4483d3bf389a37ac5a698357a72)

The top major assets that are tradeable on Solana

To access this list via shortcuts, press “2”.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets#defi-tokens)

DeFi Tokens

[Solana’s DeFi ecosystem](https://www.helius.dev/blog/solana-ecosystem-report-h1-2025)
 is home to some of crypto’s highest-revenue-generating applications, like Pump.fun, Jupiter, Kamino, Ore, and Meteora. Type “3” to navigate to the top DeFi tokens tab on Orb and view a curated list of the top assets by volume, market cap, and liquidity.

![Explore Top Defi Coins On Solana With Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/explore-top-defi-coins-on-solana-with-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=e54fe7ec6c3ba1f6df11386bfefd2bc9)

Top 10 DeFi coins tradeable on Solana

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets#tokenized-stocks)

Tokenized Stocks

xStocks powered by Backed, which Kraken recently acquired, are synthetic tokens that track the price of stocks like TSLA, NVDA, and NFLX that are traded on traditional stock exchanges like NYSE and NASDAQ. While these stocks can’t be redeemed for the underlying stock, they do use [Token Extensions](https://www.helius.dev/blog/what-is-token-2022)
, such as Scaled UI, to support stock activities like stock splits.

![Netflix Xstock On Solana With 10 1 Stock Split Token Extension Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/netflix-xstock-on-solana-with-10-1-stock-split-token-extension.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=fe37e136b8e7aca33c639bad1f8f3eec)

Netflix xStock with a new Scaled UI multiplier of 10 effective 2025-11-16 at 15:55:00 to handle Netflix’s recent 10:1 stock split

To view xStocks and PreStocks, backed by Republic Capital, click the **Stocks** tab or use the keyboard shortcut “4” to see a list of the top equities on Solana.

![Explore Top Tokenized Stocks And Equities Trading On Solana Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/explore-top-tokenized-stocks-and-equities-trading-on-solana.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=7247e6bb36eea62ec7fdd19b95feaa2a)

Top 10 xStocks and PreStocks tradeable on Solana

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets#currencies)

Currencies

Investors can also trade [stablecoins](https://www.helius.dev/blog/solanas-stablecoin-landscape)
 and foreign currencies, including stablecoins for Euros, Swiss Francs, the British Pound, and more.  To view currencies, click the **Currencies** tab or use the keyboard shortcut “5”.

![Explore Top Stablecoins And Forex Currencies On Solana With Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/explore-top-stablecoins-and-forex-currencies-on-solana-with-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=420717c0587fb2b945964e790dc4205c)

Top 10 stablecoins and Forex currencies tradeable on Solana

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets#depin-projects)

DePIN Projects

[DePIN](https://www.helius.dev/blog/a-short-introduction-to-depin)
, or Decentralized Physical Infrastructure Networks, is one of the fastest-growing sectors on Solana. On the DePIN tab, find tokens for decentralized fiber networks (DoubleZero), decentralized wireless networks (Helium), decentralized mapping (Hivemapper), and more.

![Top Solana Depin Coins Orb Explorer Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/top-solana-depin-coins-orb-explorer.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=8a830b817ac27ae523e25429a1cd1819)

Top DePIN coins tradeable on Solana

To view DePIN projects, click the **DePIN** tab or use the keyboard shortcut “6”.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets#memecoins-cults)

Memecoins (Cults)

Because of Solana’s low fees, fast transaction times, and ability to handle massive scale, it has become the blockchain of choice for memecoins.  While creators have launched millions of memecoins on Solana just this year, only a handful have developed cult-like followings, such as the official $TRUMP memecoin, which led to [historic records of trading activity on Solana](https://www.helius.dev/blog/trump-solana-memecoin-records-trends-insights)
, iconic internet memes like Popcat, and memes created by AI agents like Truth Terminal’s $FARTCOIN.

![Top Solana Memecoin Explorer Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/top-solana-memecoin-explorer-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=c29181427f6f4f112b06b6e99daf1801)

Top memecoin cult tokens tradeable on Solana

To view the top Solana memecoins, click the **Cults** tab or use the keyboard shortcut “7”.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-markets#conclusion)

**Conclusion**
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Asset discovery, research, and trading don’t need to be complicated or require multiple tools. With the [Orb block explorer](https://orb.helius.dev/)
, investors get a curated list of verified, reputable assets, key trading information like volume, market capitalization, and revenue, and a simple UI for buying any token on Solana. For more information about using Orb, check out these other tutorials:

*   [Looking Up Solana Coins](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-tokens)
    
*   [Finding Solana Token Authorities](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-authorities)
