# How to Find Top Solana Validators on Orb - Helius Docs

[Skip to main content](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#content-area)

New: getTransactionsForAddress - Query transaction history with advanced filtering, sorting, and pagination. [Learn More](https://www.helius.dev/docs/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

New: getTransactionsForAddress - Query transaction history with advanced filtering, sorting, and pagination. [Learn More](https://www.helius.dev/docs/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

[Helius Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=8dc7d328f4e40fdaa0746889c10be474)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=a2ba5e6cf5d5173b0e44b958556367d1)](https://www.helius.dev/)

![US](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/US.svg)

English

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Using Orb

How to Find Top Solana Validators on Orb

The [Orb](https://orb.helius.dev/)
 block explorer has dedicated pages for each Solana validator, with key information including vote addresses, total stake, APY, transaction history, and more. This tutorial will explain how to research Solana validators on Orb, pick [the best place to stake your SOL](https://www.helius.dev/staking/calculator)
, and begin earning [SOL staking rewards](https://www.helius.dev/staking/rewards)
.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#find-top-solana-validators)

**Find Top Solana Validators**
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two main ways to search for validators on the Orb explorer:

1.  Using the search bar
2.  From the Network section

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#searching-for-validators)

**Searching for Validators**

To find validators on Orb, simply enter their name or vote identity in the search bar. If there are multiple results for your query, filter by the “Validator” category.

![Solana Validator Explorer Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/solana-validator-explorer-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=36674656779df92a5c411e6593cc6f74)

Search for Solana validators by name or identity on the Orb explorer

Once the result appears, click it to visit their validator page.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#network-section)

**Network Section**

The [Solana network statistics](https://orb.helius.dev/stats)
 page has a summary view of the top 10 Solana validators ranked by total stake. From here, you can quickly see the top validators, sort results, and paginate through the list.

![Explore Top Solana Validators On Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/explore-top-solana-validators-on-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=3f86d6514fa8f9782d55893f68b0464c)

Explore top Solana validators on the Orb explorer network statistics page

To visit a validator page, simply click the result.

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#researching-solana-validators)

**Researching Solana Validators**
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Let’s break down the Solana validator performance metrics you can find on Orb.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#validator-stake-and-apy)

**Validator Stake and APY**

At the top of the page, you can see the validator’s total active stake, APY, commission rates, and other high-level information.

![Solana Validator Performance Explorer Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/solana-validator-performance-explorer-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=0c7625ca60b2fe4ee8aa45225be79ff8)

The validator performance metrics summary for the Helius validator on Orb

When looking for a place to stake your Solana, make sure you check the commission rates, as they directly impact how much yield you can earn. Just below the summary section, you can find some of the validator’s metadata, including:

*   **Authorized voter address:** the public key permitted to cast votes on behalf of the validator’s stake
*   **Authorized withdrawer:** the public key permitted to withdraw SOL from the stake account
*   **Identity account:** the system account that pays for vote transaction fees submitted to the vote account

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#validator-transaction-history)

**Validator Transaction History**

Below the metadata section, you’ll find a table with five different sections. These sections can be navigated using keyboard shortcuts. Simply type the numbers 1-5 to access each tab. In the **History** section, you’ll find the validator’s most recent transactions. These will mainly be votes cast on recent blocks. Click **See more details** to [inspect the transaction](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-transactions)
.

![Solana Validator Transaction History Explorer Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/solana-validator-transaction-history-explorer-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=b1281cefa5942a1e81979c52caa39bb3)

The most recent transactions executed by the Helius validator

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#validator-stake-accounts)

**Validator Stake Accounts**

Using shortcut “2”, navigate to the **Stake Accounts** section. In this table, view the account, total delegated stake, activation epoch, account creation date, and account metadata, including withdraw and stake authority.

![Solana Validator Stake Account Explorer Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/solana-validator-stake-account-explorer-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=a5f70afd85670ff5614b8a6c004db18c)

The top 10 Solana stake accounts delegated to the Helius validator

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#validator-vote-history)

**Validator Vote History**

Typing “3” on your keyboard will take you to the **Vote History** page. This page shows the most recent slots the validator voted on, along with the confirmation count. For blocks to be “rooted” on Solana, they need to receive 32 confirmations. This will give it the [“Finalized” commitment](https://www.helius.dev/blog/solana-commitment-levels)
.

![Solana Validator Vote History Explorer Orb Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS/images/solana-validator-vote-history-explorer-orb.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Mi8GsGOkm1vOOHvS&q=85&s=dcf902c95de3c6259560155c8ee7a85b)

Helius’s Solana validator vote history page on the Orb explorer

The finalization commitment levels will change with the introduction of [Alpenglow](https://www.helius.dev/blog/alpenglow)
, Solana’s upcoming consensus upgrade that replaces TowerBFT.

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#validator-delinquency-metrics)

**Validator Delinquency Metrics**

The **Delinquency** tab shows the total number of delinquent days and the total delinquent minutes over the last 12 months. You can view this in a heatmap view or as a table. Delinquent stake refers to a validator’s total stake for which it has failed to cast a vote on the network for a specified period, falling behind the cluster.  For example, [Binance’s Solana validator](https://orb.helius.dev/address/3N7s9zXMZ4QqvHQR15t5GNHyqc89KduzMP7423eWiD5g/delinquency)
 has experienced **40 delinquent days** and **651 delinquent minutes** over the past 12 months. 

![Binance Solana Validator Delinquency Metrics On The Orb Explorer Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/binance-solana-validator-delinquency-metrics-on-the-orb-explorer.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=1bf77796a75ef8762df8ef06f803b2c5)

Binance’s Solana validator delinquency heatmap on the Orb explorer

While a validator is delinquent, the validator’s stake will not earn staking rewards, which negatively impacts the SOL staking APY for delegators. When choosing a place to stake your SOL, it is important to choose a validator that is not delinquent. 

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#validator-info)

**Validator Info**

The **Info** tab shows a description of the validator along with key details such as:

*   **Identity:** the unique public key identifying the validator
*   **Stake weight:** the total amount of SOL delegated to this validator
*   **Client version:** the software version the validator is currently running
*   **Commission:** The percentage of staking rewards the validator takes as a fee
*   **Website:** a link to the validator operator’s website or informational page
*   **Location:** the geographic location of the validator’s server
*   **Network:** the provider hosting the validator’s server (e.g., Teraswitch, Latitude, etc.)
*   **ASN:** the Autonomous System Number identifying the network provider
*   **Skip rate:** the percentage of scheduled blocks the validator missed producing
*   **Vote success rate:** the percentage of valid votes the validator successfully submitted
*   **Uptime:** the duration the validator has been actively validating and voting
*   **Last vote:** the slot number of the most recent block the validator voted on
*   **First epoch:** the epoch number when the validator first began participating
*   **Root slot:** the most recent slot number the validator has finalized
*   **Epoch credits:** the number of vote credits the validator earned within the current epoch
*   **Total credits:** the cumulative number of vote credits the validator has earned all time

![Helius Solana Validator Info Section On Orb Validator Explorer Jp](https://mintcdn.com/helius/X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH/images/helius-solana-validator-info-section-on-orb-validator-explorer.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=X4NJAjNn4RMMK4jH&q=85&s=0f3536c8fa4ed15d878b7994c1a33711)

The Helius validator info tab on the Orb explorer

When selecting a place to stake SOL, look for a validator with low skip rates, high uptime, and high vote success rates, as each of these metrics will impact your total SOL yield.

*   **Uptime:** low uptime means more skipped blocks and fewer rewards
*   **Skip rates:** more skipped blocks means less issuance and MEV rewards earned
*   **Vote success rates:** lower success rates mean fewer vote credits and fewer rewards

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/orb/explore-validators#conclusion)

**Conclusion**
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The [Orb block explorer](https://orb.helius.dev/)
 is a powerful tool for researching the top validators on Solana. Once you’ve finished comparing Solana staking providers and are ready to earn yield on your SOL, start staking! If you want to stake with Helius, visit the [Orb staking portal](https://orb.helius.dev/stake)
. For more information, check out these additional staking resources:

*   [Solana Rewards](https://www.helius.dev/staking/rewards)
    
*   [SOL Staking Calculator](https://www.helius.dev/staking/calculator)
    
*   [Solana (SOL) Staking Guide](https://www.helius.dev/blog/solana-staking-simplified-guide-to-sol-staking)

Solana 历史数据概览与教程

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#%E4%B8%BA%E4%BB%80%E4%B9%88%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9-helius-%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E5%8E%86%E5%8F%B2%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E6%9F%A5%E8%AF%A2%EF%BC%9F)

为什么选择 Helius 进行历史数据查询？
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

与依赖共享 BigTable 基础设施的提供商不同，Helius 维护专用的归档节点，优化用于快速历史数据检索。这种架构为时间关键型应用提供了卓越的性能和可靠性。

独立基础设施
------

Helius 运行自己的归档系统，而不是像其他提供商那样共享 BigTable

更快的查询
-----

直接访问优化的存储意味着历史查询的响应时间更快

更高的可靠性
------

无共享基础设施瓶颈。即使在网络高峰期也能保持一致的性能

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#%E7%89%B9%E8%89%B2%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%EF%BC%9Agettransactionsforaddress)

特色方法：getTransactionsForAddress
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[高级交易历史 API\
----------\
\
我们的增强方法超越了标准 Solana RPC 功能。通过强大的过滤、双向排序和高效分页查询交易历史。**特别之处在于：**\
\
*   基于时间和槽位的过滤\
*   双向排序（最旧优先或最新优先）\
*   高效的键集分页\
*   单次请求中的完整交易数据\
*   支持版本化交易\
\
**完美适用于：**\
\
*   代币发行分析\
*   钱包历史\
*   MEV 研究\
*   合规报告\
*   投资组合跟踪](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

[查看完整文档\
------\
\
包含示例和最佳实践的完整指南](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)
[获取您的 API 密钥\
-----------\
\
今天就开始使用历史数据进行构建](https://dashboard.helius.dev/api-keys)

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E5%BD%92%E6%A1%A3%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95)

标准归档方法
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

使用这些标准 RPC 方法访问历史区块链数据。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#%E5%8C%BA%E5%9D%97%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95)

区块数据方法

查询历史区块信息和元数据。

#### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#getblock)

getBlock

检索完整的区块数据，包括特定插槽的所有交易和元数据。 **用例：**

*   区块浏览器
*   审计工具
*   历史分析

[查看 getBlock 指南\
--------------](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/guides/getblock)

#### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#getblocks)

getBlocks

获取两个插槽之间的已确认区块列表。 **用例：**

*   间隙检测
*   区块范围分析
*   索引

[查看 getBlocks 指南\
---------------](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/guides/getblocks)

#### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#getblocktime)

getBlockTime

获取区块的估计生产时间，以 Unix 时间戳表示。 **用例：**

*   基于时间的分析
*   事件关联

[查看 getBlockTime 指南\
------------------](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/guides/getblocktime)

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E5%8E%86%E5%8F%B2%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95)

交易历史方法

访问历史交易数据和签名。

#### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#gettransaction)

getTransaction

检索特定签名的完整交易详情。 **用例：**

*   交易验证
*   详细分析
*   调试

[查看 getTransaction 指南\
--------------------](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/guides/gettransaction)

#### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#getsignaturesforaddress)

getSignaturesForAddress

获取涉及某个地址的交易的已确认签名。 **用例：**

*   基本交易历史
*   签名收集

对于高级过滤和排序，请使用 [`getTransactionsForAddress`](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)
 代替。

[查看 getSignaturesForAddress 指南\
-----------------------------](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/guides/getsignaturesforaddress)

#### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#gettransactionsforaddress)

getTransactionsForAddress

增强的交易历史，具有高级过滤、双向排序和高效分页功能。**每个请求花费 100 积分。** **用例：**

*   基于时间的交易分析
*   状态过滤（成功/失败）
*   按时间顺序的历史重放
*   一次调用中获取完整的交易数据

[查看 getTransactionsForAddress 指南\
-------------------------------](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

#### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#getinflationreward)

getInflationReward

获取一个纪元中一组地址的通胀奖励。 **用例：**

*   验证者奖励
*   质押分析

[查看 getInflationReward 指南\
------------------------](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/guides/getinflationreward)

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#solana-%E5%BD%92%E6%A1%A3%E7%94%A8%E4%BE%8B)

Solana 归档用例
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

代币发行分析
------

跟踪铸币创建和早期持有者活动。识别项目起源和初始分配模式。

钱包取证
----

构建完整的交易时间线。发现资金来源和随时间变化的交易模式。

MEV 研究
------

分析历史套利和三明治攻击。研究具有精确时间数据的 MEV 机会。

合规与审计
-----

生成全面的交易报告。通过完整的历史记录支持监管合规。

投资组合跟踪
------

访问完整的 DeFi 交易历史。构建准确的投资组合分析和绩效跟踪。

区块浏览器
-----

显示完整的区块链历史。为用户提供详细的区块和交易信息。

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#%E5%8F%AF%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%86%E5%8F%B2%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E6%98%AF%E4%BB%80%E4%B9%88%EF%BC%9F)

可用的历史数据是什么？
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Helius 提供从 Solana 创世到现在的完整历史数据，并实时持续更新。我们的索引和结构化存储支持快速检索，使您能够高效查询多年的链上活动。 所有历史数据都完全支持版本化交易和所有 Solana 程序类型。Helius 在独立的归档基础设施上维护这些数据，提供一致的性能，没有共享 BigTable 系统常见的瓶颈或可靠性问题。

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/historical-data#%E5%BC%80%E5%A7%8B%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8)

开始使用
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

准备好访问 Solana 的完整历史数据了吗？以下是开始的方法：

*   **[尝试 getTransactionsForAddress](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)
    ** - 从我们的增强型交易历史 API 开始
*   **[获取您的 API 密钥](https://dashboard.helius.dev/api-keys)
    ** - 注册并开始查询历史数据
*   **[查看积分](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/billing/credits)
    ** - 查看所有方法的积分成本

# Build Your First Solana App with Helius - Helius Docs

[Skip to main content](https://www.helius.dev/docs/quickstart#content-area)

New: getTransactionsForAddress - Query transaction history with advanced filtering, sorting, and pagination. [Learn More](https://www.helius.dev/docs/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

New: getTransactionsForAddress - Query transaction history with advanced filtering, sorting, and pagination. [Learn More](https://www.helius.dev/docs/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

[Helius Docs home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=8dc7d328f4e40fdaa0746889c10be474)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/helius/RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=RGuN9Tphu9J_7kRM&q=85&s=a2ba5e6cf5d5173b0e44b958556367d1)](https://www.helius.dev/)

![US](https://d3gk2c5xim1je2.cloudfront.net/flags/US.svg)

English

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Build Your First Solana App with Helius

Ready to build on Solana? This guide will walk you through creating your first application using Helius APIs. You’ll learn how to fetch NFT data, understand the response structure, and see how easy it is to build powerful applications with our infrastructure.

1

Create Your Free Helius Account
-------------------------------

Start by creating your free account at the [Helius Dashboard](https://dashboard.helius.dev/dashboard)
. Your free tier includes 100,000 DAS API calls per month; perfect for getting started and building prototypes.

2

Get Your API Key
----------------

Navigate to the [API Keys](https://dashboard.helius.dev/api-keys)
 section and copy your key. This key gives you access to all Helius APIs, including RPC nodes, DAS API, and enhanced transaction data.

3

Make Your First API Call
------------------------

Let’s start with a practical example: fetching NFTs from a wallet. We’ll use the [getAssetsByOwner](https://www.helius.dev/docs/api-reference/das/getassetsbyowner)
 method to query assets owned by `86xCn…o2MMY` (Anatoly Yakovenko’s wallet, co-founder of Solana).**What’s happening here?** The DAS API allows you to query compressed and standard NFTs with a single call. Notice how the response includes metadata, image URLs, and ownership information - all the data you need to build rich user experiences.

4

Understanding the Response
--------------------------

Great! You’ve successfully fetched NFT data. The response includes:

*   **Asset ID**: Unique identifier for each NFT
*   **Metadata**: Name, symbol, description, and attributes
*   **Content**: Image URLs and file information
*   **Ownership**: Current owner and authority information

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/quickstart#build-it-with-code)

Build It with Code
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now let’s implement this in a real application. We’ll create a simple NFT portfolio viewer that you can expand upon.

We’ll use Node.js for this example. Make sure you have it installed from [nodejs.org](https://nodejs.org/en/download)
.

1

### Set up your project

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    mkdir solana-nft-viewer
    cd solana-nft-viewer
    npm init -y
    npm install node-fetch
    

2

### Create the NFT portfolio viewer

nft-portfolio.js

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    const fetch = require('node-fetch');
    
    class NFTPortfolioViewer {
      constructor(apiKey) {
        this.apiKey = apiKey;
        this.baseUrl = 'https://mainnet.helius-rpc.com';
      }
    
      async fetchNFTsByOwner(ownerAddress, limit = 10) {
        try {
          const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/?api-key=${this.apiKey}`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
              'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
              jsonrpc: '2.0',
              id: '1',
              method: 'getAssetsByOwner',
              params: {
                ownerAddress,
                page: 1,
                limit,
                displayOptions: {
                  showFungible: false,
                  showNativeBalance: false,
                },
              },
            }),
          });
    
          const data = await response.json();
    
          if (data.error) {
            throw new Error(data.error.message);
          }
    
          return data.result;
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Error fetching NFTs:', error.message);
          throw error;
        }
      }
    
      displayNFTPortfolio(nfts) {
        console.log('\n🖼️  NFT Portfolio Summary');
        console.log('========================');
        console.log(`Total NFTs: ${nfts.total}`);
        console.log(`Showing: ${nfts.items.length} items\n`);
    
        nfts.items.forEach((nft, index) => {
          console.log(`${index + 1}. ${nft.content?.metadata?.name || 'Unnamed NFT'}`);
          console.log(`   Collection: ${nft.grouping?.[0]?.group_value || 'Individual'}`);
          console.log(`   Compressed: ${nft.compression?.compressed ? 'Yes' : 'No'}`);
          console.log(`   Image: ${nft.content?.files?.[0]?.uri || 'No image'}`);
          console.log(`   ID: ${nft.id}\n`);
        });
      }
    
      async getRandomNFT(ownerAddress) {
        const portfolio = await this.fetchNFTsByOwner(ownerAddress, 50);
        
        if (portfolio.items.length === 0) {
          console.log('No NFTs found for this address.');
          return null;
        }
    
        const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * portfolio.items.length);
        return portfolio.items[randomIndex];
      }
    }
    
    // Usage example
    async function main() {
      const viewer = new NFTPortfolioViewer('YOUR_API_KEY');
      
      // Anatoly's wallet address
      const walletAddress = '86xCnPeV69n6t3DnyGvkKobf9FdN2H9oiVDdaMpo2MMY';
      
      console.log('🚀 Fetching NFT portfolio...');
      
      try {
        // Get full portfolio overview
        const portfolio = await viewer.fetchNFTsByOwner(walletAddress);
        viewer.displayNFTPortfolio(portfolio);
        
        // Get a random NFT for featured display
        console.log('🎲 Featured Random NFT:');
        console.log('=====================');
        const randomNFT = await viewer.getRandomNFT(walletAddress);
        
        if (randomNFT) {
          console.log(`Name: ${randomNFT.content?.metadata?.name}`);
          console.log(`Description: ${randomNFT.content?.metadata?.description || 'No description'}`);
          console.log(`Image: ${randomNFT.content?.files?.[0]?.uri}`);
        }
        
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Failed to fetch NFT data:', error.message);
      }
    }
    
    main();
    

3

### Add your API key

Replace `YOUR_API_KEY` with your actual API key from the Helius dashboard.

4

### Run your NFT portfolio viewer

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    node nft-portfolio.js
    

5

# getTransactionsForAddress 概述和教程 - Helius Docs

New: getTransactionsForAddress - Query transaction history with advanced filtering, sorting, and pagination. [Learn More](https://www.helius.dev/docs/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

New: getTransactionsForAddress - Query transaction history with advanced filtering, sorting, and pagination. [Learn More](https://www.helius.dev/docs/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress)

getTransactionsForAddress 概述和教程

**Helius 独家功能** - `getTransactionsForAddress` 仅通过 Helius RPC 节点提供，并不是标准 Solana RPC 的一部分。此端点需要 [开发者计划](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/billing/plans)
 或更高级别，并且每次请求消耗 100 积分。返回 100 个完整交易或 1,000 个签名。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E6%A6%82%E8%BF%B0)

概述
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[`getTransactionsForAddress`](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/api-reference/rpc/http/gettransactionsforaddress)
 提供强大的交易历史查询功能，具有高级过滤、灵活排序和高效分页。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E5%8A%9F%E8%83%BD)

主要功能

灵活排序
----

按时间顺序排序（最早优先）或反向排序（最新优先）

高级过滤
----

按时间范围、槽位、签名和交易状态进行过滤

完整交易数据
------

一次调用获取完整的交易详情

简单分页
----

使用 slot:position 令牌轻松分页

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E5%B8%B8%E8%A7%81%E7%94%A8%E4%BE%8B)

常见用例
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

此方法在多个场景中特别有用。**代币发行分析**有助于跟踪新项目的首次铸币交易和早期代币持有者。**钱包资金历史**允许您识别特定地址的资金来源和交易模式。**交易分析**让您可以按成功/失败状态进行过滤，专注于已完成的交易并排除失败的尝试。 该 API 还支持 **审计与合规** 工作流，通过状态过滤为特定时间段生成交易报告。**分析仪表板**可以利用历史重播功能构建全面的交易分析。最后，**投资组合跟踪**应用程序可以访问完整的成功交易历史，用于 DeFi 投资组合管理。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E6%94%AF%E6%8C%81)

网络支持
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| 网络  | 支持  | 保留期 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Mainnet | 是   | 无限  |
| Devnet | 是   | 2周  |
| Testnet | 否   | 不适用 |

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E5%BF%AB%E9%80%9F%E5%BC%80%E5%A7%8B)

快速开始
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

获取您的API密钥

从[Helius Dashboard](https://dashboard.helius.dev/api-keys)
获取您的API密钥。

2

使用高级功能查询

获取在两个日期之间的钱包的所有成功交易，按时间顺序排序：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    // Get successful transactions between Jan 1-31, 2025 in chronological order
    const response = await fetch('https://mainnet.helius-rpc.com/?api-key=YOUR_API_KEY', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        jsonrpc: '2.0',
        id: 1,
        method: 'getTransactionsForAddress',
        params: [\
          'YOUR_ADDRESS_HERE',\
          {\
            transactionDetails: 'full',\
            sortOrder: 'asc',\
            limit: 100,\
            filters: {\
              blockTime: {\
                gte: 1735689600,   // Jan 1, 2025\
                lte: 1738368000    // Jan 31, 2025\
              },\
              status: 'succeeded'  // Only successful transactions\
            }\
          }\
        ]
      })
    });
    
    const data = await response.json();
    console.log('Successful transactions in January:', data.result.data);
    

3

了解参数

此示例展示了关键功能：

*   **transactionDetails**: 设置为`'full'`以在一次调用中获取完整的交易数据
*   **sortOrder**: 使用`'asc'`按时间顺序（最旧的优先）或`'desc'`按最新的优先
*   **filters.blockTime**: 使用`gte`（大于或等于）和`lte`（小于或等于）设置时间范围
*   **filters.status**: 仅过滤`'succeeded'`或`'failed'`交易

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E5%8F%82%E6%95%B0)

请求参数
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-address)

address

string

required

要查询交易历史的账户的Base-58编码公钥

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-transaction-details)

transactionDetails

string

default:"signatures"

返回的交易详细级别：

*   `signatures`: 基本签名信息（更快）
*   `full`: 完整的交易数据（消除对getTransaction调用的需求，要求限制≤100）

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-sort-order)

sortOrder

string

default:"desc"

结果的排序顺序：

*   `desc`: 最新的优先（默认）
*   `asc`: 最旧的优先（按时间顺序，适合历史分析）

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-limit)

limit

number

default:"1000"

返回的最大交易数：

*   当`transactionDetails: "signatures"`时最多1000
*   当`transactionDetails: "full"`时最多100

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-pagination-token)

paginationToken

string

上一个响应的分页令牌（格式：`"slot:position"`）

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-commitment)

commitment

string

default:"finalized"

承诺级别：`finalized`, `confirmed`, 或 `processed`

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-filters)

filters

object

用于缩小结果范围的高级过滤选项。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-filters-slot)

filters.slot

object

使用比较运算符按槽号进行过滤：`gte`, `gt`, `lte`, `lt`示例：`{ "slot": { "gte": 1000, "lte": 2000 } }`

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-filters-block-time)

filters.blockTime

object

使用比较运算符按Unix时间戳进行过滤：`gte`, `gt`, `lte`, `lt`, `eq`示例：`{ "blockTime": { "gte": 1640995200, "lte": 1641081600 } }`

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-filters-signature)

filters.signature

object

使用比较运算符按交易签名进行过滤：`gte`, `gt`, `lte`, `lt`示例：`{ "signature": { "lt": "SIGNATURE_STRING" } }`

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-filters-status)

filters.status

string

按交易成功/失败状态进行过滤：

*   `succeeded`: 仅成功的交易
*   `failed`: 仅失败的交易
*   `any`: 成功和失败的交易（默认）

示例：`{ "status": "succeeded" }`

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-encoding)

encoding

string

交易数据的编码格式（仅在`transactionDetails: "full"`时适用）。与`getTransaction` API相同。选项：`json`, `jsonParsed`, `base64`, `base58`

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-max-supported-transaction-version)

maxSupportedTransactionVersion

number

设置要返回的最大交易版本。如果省略，将仅返回传统交易。设置为`0`以包含所有版本的交易。

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#param-min-context-slot)

minContextSlot

number

请求可以评估的最小槽位

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E8%BF%87%E6%BB%A4%E8%BF%90%E7%AE%97%E7%AC%A6)

过滤运算符
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

使用过滤器时，可以使用比较运算符进行`slot`, `blockTime`或`signature`，以及一个特殊的`status`过滤器。这些运算符的工作方式类似于数据库查询，能够精确控制数据范围。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E6%AF%94%E8%BE%83%E8%BF%90%E7%AE%97%E7%AC%A6)

比较运算符

| 运算符 | 全名  | 描述  | 示例  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `gte` | 大于或等于 | 包含值 ≥ 指定值 | `slot: { gte: 100 }` |
| `gt` | 大于  | 包含值 > 指定值 | `blockTime: { gt: 1641081600 }` |
| `lte` | 小于或等于 | 包含值 ≤ 指定值 | `slot: { lte: 2000 }` |
| `lt` | 小于  | 包含值 < 指定值 | `blockTime: { lt: 1641168000 }` |
| `eq` | 等于  | 包含值完全等于（仅`blockTime`） | `blockTime: { eq: 1641081600 }` |

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E7%8A%B6%E6%80%81%E8%BF%87%E6%BB%A4%E5%99%A8)

状态过滤器

| 过滤器 | 描述  | 值   |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `status` | 按成功/失败过滤交易 | `succeeded`, `failed`, 或 `any` |

**组合过滤器示例：**

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    // Time range with successful transactions only
    "filters": {
      "blockTime": {
        "gte": 1640995200,
        "lte": 1641081600
      },
      "status": "succeeded"
    }
    
    // Slot range
    "filters": {
      "slot": {
        "gte": 1000,
        "lte": 2000
      }
    }
    
    // Only failed transactions
    "filters": {
      "status": "failed"
    }
    

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E5%93%8D%E5%BA%94%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F)

响应格式
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   签名响应
    
*   完整交易响应
    

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "jsonrpc": "2.0",
      "id": 1,
      "result": {
        "data": [\
          {\
            "signature": "5h6xBEauJ3PK6SWCZ1PGjBvj8vDdWG3KpwATGy1ARAXFSDwt8GFXM7W5Ncn16wmqokgpiKRLuS83KUxyZyv2sUYv",\
            "slot": 1054,\
            "err": null,\
            "memo": null,\
            "blockTime": 1641038400,\
            "confirmationStatus": "finalized"\
          }\
        ],
        "paginationToken": "1055:5"
      }
    }
    

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "jsonrpc": "2.0", 
      "id": 1,
      "result": {
        "data": [\
          {\
            "slot": 1054,\
            "transaction": {\
              "signatures": ["5h6xBEauJ3PK6SWCZ1PGjBvj8vDdWG3KpwATGy1ARAXFSDwt8GFXM7W5Ncn16wmqokgpiKRLuS83KUxyZyv2sUYv"],\
              "message": {\
                "accountKeys": ["...", "..."],\
                "instructions": [...],\
                // Complete transaction structure\
              }\
            },\
            "meta": {\
              "fee": 5000,\
              "preBalances": [1000000, 2000000],\
              "postBalances": [999995000, 2000000],\
              // Complete metadata\
            }\
          }\
        ],
        "paginationToken": "1055:5"
      }
    }
    

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E7%A4%BA%E4%BE%8B)

实用示例
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E5%9F%BA%E4%BA%8E%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90)

基于时间的分析

生成每月交易报告：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    // Get all successful transactions for January 2025
    const startTime = Math.floor(new Date('2025-01-01').getTime() / 1000);
    const endTime = Math.floor(new Date('2025-02-01').getTime() / 1000);
    
    {
      "jsonrpc": "2.0",
      "id": 1,
      "method": "getTransactionsForAddress",
      "params": [\
        "WALLET_OR_PROGRAM_ADDRESS",\
        {\
          "transactionDetails": "signatures",\
          "filters": {\
            "blockTime": {\
              "gte": startTime,\
              "lt": endTime\
            },\
            "status": "succeeded"\
          },\
          "limit": 1000\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

分析处理：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    // Calculate daily transaction volume
    const dailyStats = {};
    response.result.data.forEach(tx => {
      const date = new Date(tx.blockTime * 1000).toISOString().split('T')[0];
      dailyStats[date] = (dailyStats[date] || 0) + 1;
    });
    
    console.log('Daily Transaction Counts:', dailyStats);
    

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E4%BB%A3%E5%B8%81%E9%93%B8%E9%80%A0%E5%88%9B%E5%BB%BA)

代币铸造创建

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "jsonrpc": "2.0",
      "id": "find-first-mints",
      "method": "getTransactionsForAddress",
      "params": [\
        MINT_ADDRESS, // Token mint address\
        {\
          "encoding": "jsonParsed",\
          "maxSupportedTransactionVersion": 0,\
          "sortOrder": "asc",  // Chronological order from the beginning\
          "limit": 10,\
          "transactionDetails": "full"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

对于流动性池创建，查询池地址：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "jsonrpc": "2.0",
      "id": 1,
      "method": "getTransactionsForAddress", 
      "params": [\
        "POOL_ADDRESS_HERE", // Raydium/Meteora pool address\
        {\
          "transactionDetails": "full",\
          "sortOrder": "asc",  // First transaction is usually pool creation\
          "limit": 1\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

**用例**：查找代币铸造或流动性池创建的确切时刻，包括创建者地址和初始参数。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E8%B5%84%E9%87%91%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93)

资金交易

查找谁为特定地址提供资金：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "jsonrpc": "2.0",
      "id": 1,
      "method": "getTransactionsForAddress",
      "params": [\
        "TARGET_WALLET_ADDRESS",\
        {\
          "transactionDetails": "full",\
          "sortOrder": "asc",  // Oldest first\
          "limit": 10\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

然后分析交易数据以查找SOL转账：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    response.result.data.forEach(tx => {
      // Look for SOL transfers in preBalances/postBalances
      const balanceChanges = tx.meta.preBalances.map((pre, index) => 
        tx.meta.postBalances[index] - pre
      );
      
      // Positive balance change = incoming SOL
      balanceChanges.forEach((change, index) => {
        if (change > 0) {
          console.log(`Received ${change} lamports from ${tx.transaction.message.accountKeys[index]}`);
        }
      });
    });
    

前几笔交易通常会揭示资金来源，并有助于识别相关地址或资金模式。

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E5%88%86%E9%A1%B5)

分页
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

当交易数量超过限制时，使用响应中的`paginationToken`获取下一页。该令牌是一个简单的字符串，格式为`"slot:position"`，告诉API从哪里继续。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E5%A6%82%E4%BD%95%E5%88%86%E9%A1%B5)

如何分页

使用每个响应中的分页令牌获取下一页：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    // First request
    let paginationToken = null;
    let allTransactions = [];
    
    const getNextPage = async (paginationToken = null) => {
      const params = [\
        'ADDRESS',\
        {\
          transactionDetails: 'signatures',\
          limit: 100,\
          ...(paginationToken && { paginationToken })\
        }\
      ];
    
      const response = await fetch(rpcUrl, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          jsonrpc: '2.0',
          id: 1,
          method: 'getTransactionsForAddress',
          params
        })
      });
    
      const data = await response.json();
      return data.result;
    };
    
    // Paginate through all results
    do {
      const result = await getNextPage(paginationToken);
      allTransactions.push(...result.data);
      paginationToken = result.paginationToken;
      
      console.log(`Fetched ${result.data.length} transactions, total: ${allTransactions.length}`);
    } while (paginationToken);
    

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E5%A4%9A%E4%B8%AA%E5%9C%B0%E5%9D%80)

多个地址

您不能在单个请求中查询多个地址。要获取多个地址的交易，请在相同的时间或槽窗口内查询每个地址，然后合并和排序：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    const addresses = ['Address1...', 'Address2...', 'Address3...'];
    
    // Query all addresses in parallel with slot filter
    const results = await Promise.all(
      addresses.map(address => 
        fetch(rpcUrl, {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            jsonrpc: '2.0',
            id: 1,
            method: 'getTransactionsForAddress',
            params: [address, {\
              sortOrder: 'desc',\
              filters: { slot: { gt: 250000000 } }\
            }]
          })
        }).then(r => r.json())
      )
    );
    
    // Merge and sort by slot
    const allTransactions = results
      .flatMap(r => r.result.data)
      .sort((a, b) => b.slot - a.slot);
    

对于较大的历史扫描，通过时间或槽窗口迭代（例如，每次1000个槽）并重复此模式。

每个地址查询都算作一个单独的API请求（每个地址100个积分）。

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E6%9C%80%E4%BD%B3%E5%AE%9E%E8%B7%B5)

最佳实践
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E6%80%A7%E8%83%BD)

性能

为了获得最佳性能，当不需要完整交易数据时，使用`transactionDetails: "signatures"`。实现合理的页面大小以获得更好的响应时间，并考虑按时间范围或特定槽进行过滤以进行更有针对性的查询。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E8%BF%87%E6%BB%A4)

过滤

从广泛的过滤器开始，然后逐步缩小范围以找到所需的数据。使用基于时间的过滤器进行分析和报告工作流。您可以结合多个过滤器进行精确查询，以定位特定的交易类型或时间段。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E5%88%86%E9%A1%B5-2)

分页

在需要稍后恢复大型查询时存储分页键。监控分页深度以进行性能规划，并在需要按时间顺序重放历史事件的情况下使用升序。

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E9%94%99%E8%AF%AF%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86)

错误处理

使用指数退避策略优雅地处理速率限制。在发出请求之前始终验证地址，并在适当时缓存结果以减少API使用并提高应用程序性能。

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E8%BF%99%E4%B8%8Egetsignaturesforaddress%E6%9C%89%E4%BD%95%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%9F)

这与getSignaturesForAddress有何不同？
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

如果您熟悉标准`getSignaturesForAddress`方法，这里是主要区别：

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E4%B8%80%E6%AC%A1%E8%B0%83%E7%94%A8%E8%8E%B7%E5%8F%96%E5%AE%8C%E6%95%B4%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93)

一次调用获取完整交易

使用`getSignaturesForAddress`，您需要两个步骤：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    // Step 1: Get signatures
    const signatures = await connection.getSignaturesForAddress(address, { limit: 100 });
    
    // Step 2: Get transaction details (100 additional calls!)
    const transactions = await Promise.all(
      signatures.map(sig => connection.getTransaction(sig.signature))
    );
    

使用`getTransactionsForAddress`，只需一次调用：

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    const response = await fetch(heliusRpcUrl, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        jsonrpc: '2.0',
        id: 1,
        method: 'getTransactionsForAddress',
        params: [\
          address,\
          {\
            transactionDetails: 'full',\
            limit: 100\
          }\
        ]
      })
    });
    

### 

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E9%A2%9D%E5%A4%96%E5%8A%9F%E8%83%BD)

额外功能

按时间顺序排序
-------

使用`sortOrder: 'asc'`将交易从最旧排序到最新

基于时间的过滤
-------

使用`blockTime`过滤器按时间范围过滤

状态过滤
----

使用`status`过滤器仅获取成功或失败的交易

更简单的分页
------

使用`paginationToken`代替复杂的`before`/`until`签名

* * *

[​](https://www.helius.dev/docs/zh/rpc/gettransactionsforaddress#%E6%94%AF%E6%8C%81%E4%B8%8E%E7%A4%BE%E5%8C%BA)
